**ardha-nārī-nara-vapuḥ pracaṇḍo’tiśarīravān |**  
**vibhajātmānam ity uktvā taṁ brahmāntardadhe tataḥ ||13||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** nava brahmāṇa iti || purāṇe-brahmāṁḍādau | pūrvaṁ sṛṣṭeḥ ||6-13|| 

**tathokto’sau dvidhā strītvaṁ puruṣatvaṁ tathākarot |**  
**vibheda-puruṣatvaṁ ca daśadhā caikadhā punaḥ ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: arddhābhyāṁ nārī ca naraś ca vapuryasya saḥ | pracaṇḍaḥ atikrodhanaḥ | ātmānaṁ strīpuruṣākāradehaṁ vibhajya, pṛthak kuru iti tam uktvā antardhānaṁ gataḥ ||13-14||

**saumyāsaumyais tadā śāntāśāntaiḥ strītvaṁ ca sa prabhuḥ |**  
**vibheda bahudhā devaḥ svarūpair asitaiḥ sitaiḥ ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: saumyāsaumyaiḥ ityasyaiva vivaraṇaṁ śāntāśāntai rūpairiti ||15||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tayoktā iti || strītvaṁ puruṣatvaṁ ca dvidhā akarot-pṛthak cakāra | puṁstvaṁ caikādaśavidhaṁ rūpamedaiḥ ||14-15||

**tato brahmātma-sambhūtaṁ pūrvaṁ svāyambhuvaṁ prabhuḥ |**  
**ātmānam eva kṛtavān prajāpālye manuṁ dvija ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tata ekādaśavibhāgataḥ krodhāṁśe nirgate sati sāttvikasvabhāvaṁ pūrvam ātmānaḥ svadehāt sambhūtam ata eva ātmā vai putrānāmāsi iti śruterātmānam eva ta manuṁ prajāpālanārthamakarodity arthaḥ ||16||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tata iti || ātmasaṁbhūtam | ata eva svāyaṁbhuvam ātmānam eva taṁ prajāpālye nimitte pūrvaṁ manuṁ kṛtavān ||16||

**śatarūpāṁ ca tāṁ nārīṁ tapo-nirdhūta-kalmaṣām |**  
**svāyambhuvo manur devaḥ patnītve jagṛhe prabhuḥ ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tāṁ svadehārddhabhūtānāṁ nārīṁ patnyarthaṁ jagṛhe | tapasānidhūrtakalmaṣām iti ca, deva iti ca, vibhuriti ca, sāpiṇḍyadoṣaparihārārthamuktam ||17|| 

**tasmāt tu puruṣād devī śatarūpā vyajāyata |**  
**priyavartottānapādau prasūtyākūti-saṁjñitam ||18||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** śatarūpām iti || śatarūpām-arddhena puruṣo'bhavadarddhena nārītyuktāyā brahmapatnyāḥ śatarūpāyā aṁśabhūtāṁ brahmāṁśabhūto manurjagṛhe ||17-18||

**kanyā-dvayaṁ ca dharmajña rūpaudārya-guṇānvitam |**  
**dadau prasūtiṁ dakṣāya ākūtiṁ rucaye purā ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vyajāyata prasūtā ||18-19|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** kanyāvayam iti || prajāpatirākūtiṁ rucaye dadau ||19||

**prajāpatiḥ sa jagrāha tayor jajñe sa-dakṣiṇaḥ |**  
**putro yajño mahābhāga dampatyor mithunaṁ tataḥ ||20||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sa ca ruciḥ tāṁ jagrāha | tayor dakṣiṇāsahito yajño mithunam eva putro jajñe || prajāpatiriti || saḥ-ruciḥjagrāha; tayoḥ-ākūtirucyordampatthoḥ sadakṣiṇo yajñaḥ putro mithunaṁ jajñe ||20|| 

**yajñasya dakṣiṇāyāṁ tu putrā dvādaśa jajñire |**  
**yāmā iti samākhyātā devāḥ svāyambhuve manau ||21||**

**prasūtyāṁ ca tathā dakṣaś catasro viṁśatis tathā |**  
**sasarja kanyās tāsāṁ ca samyaṅ nāmāni me śṛṇu ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: svāyambhuve manau tanmanvantare yāmā iti devāḥ samākhyātāḥ ||21-22|| 

**śraddhā lakṣmīr dhṛtis tuṣṭir medhā puṣṭis tathā kriyā |**  
**buddhir lajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtis trayodaśī ||23||**

**patny-arthaṁ pratijagrāha dharmo dākṣāyiṇīḥ prabhuḥ |**  
**tābhyaḥ śiṣṭā yavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ ||24||**

**khyātiḥ saty atha sambhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamā tathā |**  
**santatiś cānasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā ||25||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tāsāṁ nāmāni kathayanneva vivāhānāha—śraddhā ity-ādipañcabhiḥ ||23-25||

**bhṛgur bhavo marīciś ca tathā caivāṅgirā muniḥ |**  
**pulastyaḥ pulahaś caiva kratuś ca rṣi-varas tathā ||26||**

**atrir vasiṣṭho vahniś ca pitaraś ca yathā-kramam |**  
**khyāty-ādyā jagṛhuḥ kanyā munayo muni-sattama ||27||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** yajñasyeti || svāyaṁbhuve mano-manvantare ||21-27||

**śraddhā kāmaṁ calā darpaṁ niyamaṁ dhṛtir ātmajam |**  
**santoṣaṁ ca tathā tuṣṭir lobhaṁ puṣṭir asūyata ||28||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dharmapatnīnāṁ trayodaśānāṁ putrānāha—śraddhā iti tribhiḥ | calā lakṣmīḥ ||28|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** śraddheti || śraddhā kāmaṁ tathā darpam iti pāṭhe tathetyanena kramaprāptā lakṣmīrlakṣyā | yathā kaurme śraddhāyāstu sutaḥ kāmo darpo lakṣmyāssutassmṛtaḥ iti ||28||

**medhā śrutaṁ kriyā daṇḍaṁ nayaṁ vinayam eva ca ||29||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** megheti || kriyā daṇḍam-kiyāyāṁ tāmasyāṁ daṇḍaḥ, rājasyāṁ nayaḥ, sāttvikyāṁ mānaso'nauddhatyātmā vinayaḥ ||29||

**bodhaṁ buddhis tathā lajjā vinayaṁ vapur ātmajam |**  
**vyavasāyaṁ prajajñe vai kṣemaṁ śāntir asūyata ||30||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kriyā triguṇā, ataḥ tamo'śena daṇḍa, rajoṁ'śena nayaṁ, sattvāṁśena vinayam anauddhatyarūpam asūyat | lajjā śarīraṁ vinayaṁ, vapuḥsaṁjñā vyavasāyātmakaṁ prajajñe ||30|| 

**sukhaṁ siddhir yaśaḥ kīrtir ity ete dharma-sūnavaḥ |**  
**kāmād ratiḥ sutaṁ harṣaṁ dharma-pautram asūyata ||31||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kīrtiryaśaḥsaṁjñaṁ putramasūyata ||31|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** bodham iti || lajjnāyāstu śārīro vinayaḥ ||30-31||

**hiṁsā bhāryā tv adharmasya tato jajñe tathānṛtam |**  
**kanyā ca nikṛtis tābhyām bhayaṁ narakam eva ca ||32||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: nandā kāmasya bhāryā | tad evaṁ dharmabhāryāṇāṁ vaṁśā uktāḥ, anyāsāṁ dakṣakanyānāṁ putrān devau dhātā-vidhātārau bhṛgoḥ khyātir asūyata ity-ādinā uttarādhyāyatraye vakṣyati | tatra tāvad dharmavaṁśoktyā tatpratiyogitayā ca buddhisthasya adharmasya vaṁśaṁ prasaktānuprasaktena ca nityapralayādikam āha—hiṁsā ity-ādinā | dharmādharmau ca brahmaṇaḥ putrau | 

dharmaḥ stanād dakṣiṇato yatra nārāyaṇaḥ svayam |   
adharmaḥ pṛṣṭhato yasmāt mṛtyulokabhayaṅkaraḥ iti śukokteḥ

nikṛtirvañcanaṁ tābhyāmanṛtanikṛtibhyāṁ bhaya-narakākhyaṁ putradvayaṁ jajñe ||32||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** dharmaprasaṅgādadharmasargam āha—hiṁseti || tayoḥ-adharmahiṁsayoḥ, anṛtaṁ nikṛtiś ca jajñe, tābhyāṁ nikṛtyanṛtābhyāṁ māyā bhayaṁ vedanā narakaṁ ca jajñe ||32||

**māyā ca vedanā caiva mithunaṁ tv idam etayoḥ |**  
**tayor jajñe’tha vai māyā mṛtyuṁ bhūtāpahāriṇam ||33||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: etayos tu bhaya-narakayor yathā-kramaṁ māyā ca vedanā ceti mithunatva-sampādakaṁ bhāryād vayaṁ ca tābhyām eva jajñe ity arthaḥ | tayor māyā-vedanayor madhye māyā mṛtyuṁ jajñe janayāmāsa bhayād ity artha-siddham ||33||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** māyeti || tasmād etayor mithuna-dvayam, bhayāj jajña iti pāṭhe etayor mithunayor madhye māyā bhayāt tu mṛtyuṁ jajñe | “tayor jajñe” iti pāṭhe māyā mṛtyuṁ suṣuve, bhayād iti śeṣaḥ ||33||

**vedanā sva-sutaṁ cāpi duḥkhaṁ jajñe’tha rauravāt |**  
**mṛtyor vyādhi-jarā-śoka-tṛṣṇā-krodhāś ca jajñire ||34||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vedanā ca duḥkhaṁ sva-sutaṁ sva-yogyaṁ sutaṁ rauravān narakāj janayāmāsety arthaḥ ||34|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** vedaneti || rauravāt-bhayaṁ narakam eva cety uktān narakāt ||34||

**duḥkhottarāḥ smṛtā hy ete sarve cādharma-lakṣaṇāḥ |**  
**naiṣāṁ putro’sti vai bhāryā te sarve hy ūrdhva-retasaḥ ||35||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: duḥkhottarā duḥkhedarkā yato'dharmalakṣaṇāḥ pāparūpāḥ | yadvā prācīnādharmajñāpakāḥ, tatphalatvādeṣāṁ vyādhyādīnām | ūrdhvaretasaḥ kāryānutpādakāḥ caramakāryaduḥkhabhogātpakatvāt ||35|| 

**raudrāṇy etāni rūpāṇi viṣṇor muni-varātmaja |**  
**nitya-pralaya-hetutvaṁ jagato’sya prayānti vai ||36||**

**dakṣo marīcir atriś ca bhṛgv-ādyāś ca prajeśvarāḥ |**  
**jagaty atra mahābhāga nitya-sargasya hetavaḥ ||37||**

**manavo manu-putrāś ca bhūpā vīrya-dharāś ca ye |**  
**sanmārga-niratāḥ śūrās te sarve sthiti-kāriṇaḥ ||38||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** duḥkhottarā iti || adharmalakṣaṇāḥ-adharmo vaṁśamūlabhūto lakṣaṇaṁ yeṣāṁ te tathoktāḥ | te-vyādhyādyāḥ, ūrdhvaretasaḥ-caramakāryasya duḥkhātmakatvākāryāntarānutpādakāḥ ||35-38||

**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**  
**yena nityā sthitir brahman nitya-sargas tatheritaḥ |**  
**nityābhāvaś ca teṣāṁ vai svarūpaṁ mama kathyatām ||39||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: nityapralayahetuprasaṅgānnityasarganityasthitihetūnāha—dakṣa iti dvābhyām ||

nanu manvādīnāṁ kādācitkānāṁ kathaṁ nityasthity-ādihetutvam ity āśayena pṛcchati yeyam iti | nityābhāvāḥ-nityapralayāḥ ||39||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** jīvānāṁ sṛjyatvādinā pārataṁtryānnityasargādau hetutvamanupapannam ity āśaṅkya tatparihārabubhutsayā teṣāṁ svarūpaṁ pṛcchati-yeyam iti ||39||

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**sarga-sthiti-vināśāṁś caiva bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ |**  
**tais tai rūpair acintyātmā karoty avyāhato vibhuḥ ||40||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: taistairdakṣādimanvādirūpairbhagavāneva sargādīn karoti, ato na uktadoṣaprasaṅga ity arthaḥ | avyahatān avicchinnān ||40||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** viṣṇur eva sattvādiśaktyādhānadvārā taistairmanyādirūpaiḥ sthity-ādi karotīti pariharati-sargeti || testaiḥ-manvādirūpaiḥ | manvādayaḥ sattvasthāḥ, dakṣādayo rājasāḥ, vyādhyādayastāmasāḥ ||40||

**naimittikaḥ prākṛtikas tathaivātyantiko dvija |**  
**nityaś ca sarva-bhūtānāṁ pralayo’yaṁ caturvidhaḥ ||41||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tatra pralayaṁ caturdhā prapañcayati-naimittika iti tribhiḥ ||41||

**brāhmo naimittikas tatra śete’yaṁ jagatīpatiḥ |**  
**prayāti prākṛte caiva brahmāṇḍaṁ prakṛtau layam ||42||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yacchete yadā śete | brahmanidrānimitto naimittikaḥ | brahmāṇḍaṁ yadā prakṛtau layaṁ prayāti, sa prākṛtika ity arthaḥ ||42||

**jñānād ātyantikaḥ prokto yoginaḥ paramātmani |**  
**nityaḥ sadaiva bhūtānāṁ yo vināśo divā-niśam ||43||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: jñānāt paramātmani yogino laya ātyantikaḥ, sadaiva dīpajvālāvat sāntatyena jātānāṁ divāniśaṁ yo vināśaḥ sa nityaḥ ||43||

**prasūtiḥ prakṛter yā tu sā sṛṣṭiḥ prākṛtā smṛtā |**  
**dainandinī tathā proktā yāntara-pralayād anu ||44||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: trividhāṁ sṛṣṭim āha—prasūtir iti mahāpralayāvasāne prakṛteḥ sakāśād yā mahadādiprasatiḥ, sā prākṛtī sṛṣṭiḥ | avāntarapralayādanantaraṁ yā carācarasṛṣṭiḥ, sā dainandinī ||44||

**bhūtāny anudinaṁ yatra jāyante muni-sattama |**  
**nitya-sargo hi sa proktaḥ purāṇārtha-vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||45||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: bhūtānīti-asmadādisṛṣṭipravāho nityasarga ity arthaḥ | ātyantikapralayavadātyantikasṛṣṭerabhāvāt sṛṣṭistrividhaiva ||45|| 

**evaṁ sarva-śarīreṣu bhagavān bhūta-bhāvanaḥ |**  
**saṁsthitaḥ kurute viṣṇur utpatti-sthiti-saṁyamān ||46||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: upasaṁharati-evam iti ||46||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** atha nityapralayasya svarūpaṁ darśayan prasaṁgātpralayasya cāturvidhyam āha—naimittika ity-ādinā | naimitika iti | ātyantika iti | naimittikādilayeṣu suṣuptyutkrāntyoś ca jīvasya paramātmani laye'pi karmakṣayābhāvāt punarbhavo vidyate | ātyantike tu niśśeṣakarmāvidyādināśānna punarbhava iti viśeṣaḥ ||41-46|| 

**sṛṣṭi-sthiti-vināśānāṁ śaktayaḥ sarva-dehiṣu |**  
**vaiṣṇavyaḥ parivartante maitreyāhar-niśaṁ samāḥ ||47||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tarhi viṣṇoḥ sarvaśarīreṣu sarvadā sthitatvāt kālabhedena utpattyādayo na syuḥ tatrāha—sṛṣṭi iti | tathāpi viṣṇuśaktīnāṁ sattvādīnāṁ tatra tatra kālabhedena sañcārātrāyaṁ doṣa iti bhāvaḥ ||47||

**guṇa-traya-mayaṁ hy etad brahman śakti-trayaṁ mahat |**  
**yo’tiyāti sa yāty eva paraṁ nāvartate punaḥ ||48||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yasmāt triguṇātmakaviṣṇuśaktitraparivṛtyā sṛṣṭyādipravāho bhavati, ato guṇātītasya na punastatpravāhapāta ityāha-guṇatraya iti | yo'tiyāti atikrāmati, sa paraṁ padaṁ yātyeva na punarāvarttate iti śruteḥ ||45|| 

iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśābhidhāyāṁ viṣṇu purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ prathamāṁśe 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** sṛṣṭīti || vaiṣṇavyaḥ-viṣṇusaṁkalpānuvartinyaḥ śaktayaḥ sattvādyāḥ, aharniśam-sadā avicchedena | sarvo'pi jano viṣṇuśaktipreritaḥ kālabhedādviṣayabhedācca sargādi karoti ||47-48||

iti śrī viṣṇu-purāṇavyākhyāne viṣṇucitīye prathame'ṁśe saptamo'dhyāyaḥ ||7||

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe prathame’ṁśe saptamo’dhyāyaḥ   
||7||

—o)0(o—

(1.8)



## **lakṣmy-utpatti-kathanaṁ**

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**kathitas tāmasaḥ sargo brahmaṇas te mahā-mune |**  
**rudra-sargaṁ pravakṣyāmi tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dakṣa-jāmātur dharmasya vaṁśoktau tat-pratiyogitayā buddhi-sthasyādharmasya nitya-pralaya-hetuṁ tāmasaṁ vaṁśam uktvā, idānīṁ tad-anuvāda-pūrvakaṁ prastutaṁ dakṣa-kanyā-dvayam anuvartayitum tat-kanyā-pariṇetur nīlalohita-rudrasya sargam āha—kathita iti | yadyap khyātiḥ saty atha sambhūtiḥ ity upadeśa-krameṇa khyāter anvayaḥ | prathamaṁ vaktuṁ yuktaḥ, tathāpi tat-kathā ativitatatvād anantaraṁ vakṣyate | yad vā, pūrvoktāt tāmasād rudra-sargād anyo’yaṁ kumāra-sargāntar-bhūtaḥ sāttviko rudra-sargaḥ | tam imaṁ śṛṇuṣva iti sambandhaḥ ||1||

**kalpādāv ātmanas tulyaṁ sutaṁ pradhyāyatas tataḥ |**  
**prādurāsīt prabhor aṅke kumāro nīlalohitaḥ ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: rudan dravaṁś ca prādurāsīd iti rudra-nāma-niruktiḥ | 

evam uktās tu rurudur drudruvuś ca samantataḥ |  
rodanād dravaṇāc caiva rudrā nāmneti viśrutāḥ || iti vāyūkteḥ ||2||

**rudan vai susvaraṁ so’tha dravaṁś ca dvija-sattama |**  
**kiṁ rodiṣīta taṁ brahmā rudantaṁ pratyuvāca ha ||3||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** nityapralayahetoradharmādestāmasatya prasaṅgādbhṛgusargamatikamya pūrvoktakaumārasargāntargataṁ tāmasaṁ rudrasargaṁ prapañcayituṁ prastauti kathita iti ||1-3|| 

**nāma dehīti taṁ so’tha pratyuvāca prajāpatim |**  
**rudras tvaṁ deva nāmnāsi mā rodīr dhairyam āvaha ||4||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: he deva \! tvaṁ rudro’si rodanād dravaṇāc cety  arthaḥ ||4||

**evam uktaḥ punaḥ so’tha sapta-kṛtvo ruroda vai |**  
**tato’nyāni dadau tasmai sapta nāmāni vai prabhuḥ |**  
**sthānāni caiṣām aṣṭānāṁ patnīḥ putrāṁs ca vai prabhuḥ ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: parameśvarasyāpi sato rodanādi śiśutva-nāṭyaṁ loka-saṅgrahāya pitṛ-pāratantrya-dyotanārtham | ata eva āścaryatvād rodanāder nāma-nirukta-hetutvād rodanādi-nāmopādhi-bhedād aṣṭānām ity ucyate ||5|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** nāmeti || rodanadravaṇābhyāṁ rudranāmaniruktiḥ | rodanāddravaṇāccaiva rudranāmnāmiviśrutaḥ iti vāyūkteḥ ||4-5|| 

**bhavaṁ sarvaṁ maheśānaṁ tathā paśupatiṁ dvija |**  
**bhīmam ugraṁ mahādevam uvāca sa pitāmahaḥ ||6||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: anyāni sapta nāmāni dadāv ity uktam | tāny evāha—bhavam iti | taṁ bhavādi-nāmānam uvāca—tasya bhavādi-nāmāni kṛtavān ity arthaḥ ||6||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tata iti || nāmāni-rudrabhavādīni, patnīḥ-suvarcalādikāḥ ||5-6||

**cakre nāmāny athaitāni sthānāny eṣāṁ cakāra saḥ |**  
**sūryo jalaṁ mahī vahnir vāyur ākāśam eva ca |**  
**dīkṣito brāhmaṇaḥ soma ity etās tanavaḥ kramāt ||7||**  
**suvarcalā tathavomā sukeśī cāparā śivā |**  
**svāhā diśas tathā dīkṣā rohiṇī ca yathā-kramam ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tad evāha—cakre nāmāni | rudra-bhavādīnāṁ sūryādīni aṣṭa sthānāni | tāny eva abhivyakti-sthānatvāt tanavo mūrtaya ucyante | dīkṣito brāhmaṇa iti sa-dharmānuṣṭhātari kṣetrajñe paramātmābhivyakes tan-mūrtitvam | 

ātmā tasyāṣṭamī mūrtiḥ śivasya paramātmaḥ |  
vyāīketara-mūrtīnāṁ viśvaṁ tasmāc chivātmakam ||  
sthāeṣv eteṣu ye rudraṁ dhyāyanti praṇamanti ca |  
teṣām aṣṭa-tanur devo dadāti paramaṁ padam || iti vāyūkteḥ |

sūryo jalaṁ mahī vāyur vahnir iti kramo draṣṭavyaḥ | tathā sati suvarcalādīnāṁ patnīnāṁ yathā-kramam sambandhaḥ | vāyoḥ śivā patnī | vahneḥ svāheti sidhyati | vakṣyamāṇe’pi putra-krame vahneḥ skandaḥ putra iti upapatsyate, ato vahnir vāyur iti pāṭha-kramo na vivakṣitaḥ ||7-8||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** cakre nāmānīti || atra vahnirvāyuriti pāṭhakramo na vivakṣitaḥ, agnerdevatāpatnīputrāṇāṁ paśupati svāhāskandānāṁ paṁcamasthāne vakṣyamāṇatvāt ||7-8||

**sūryādīnāṁ nara-śreṣṭha rudrādyair nāmabhiḥ saha |**  
**patnyaḥ smṛtā mahā-bhāga tad-apatyāni me śṛṇu |**  
**yeṣāṁ sūti-prasūtair vā idam āpūritaṁ jagat ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sūti-prasūtairḥ putraiḥ pautrādibhiś ca ||9||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** sūryādīnām iti || sūryādīnāṁ-rudramūrtīnām ||9|| 

**śanaiścaras tathā śukro lohitāṅgo manojavaḥ |**  
**skandaḥ khargo’tha santāno budhaś cānukramāt sutāḥ ||10||**  
**evaṁ-prakāro rudro’sau satīṁ bhāryām avindata |**  
**dakṣa-kopāc ca tatyāja sā satī svaṁ kalevaram ||11||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uktasya rudra-sargasya prastutopayogam āha—evam-prakāra iti | satīṁ nāma dakṣasya kanyām, dakṣa-kopāt pitrā dakṣeṇa sva-yajñe rudra-varjanodbhūtāt | atas tasyāḥ santatir nābhūd iti bhāvaḥ ||11||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** eṣām iti || sūtipramūnibhyām-mūtiḥ-putrādiḥ, prasūtiḥ-pautrādiḥ ||10-11||

**himavad duhitā sābhūn menāyāṁ dvija-sattama |**  
**upayeme punaś comām ananyāṁ bhagavān bhavaḥ ||12||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ananyāṁ bhavaika-niṣṭhām ||12||

**devau dhātṛ-vidhātārau bhṛgoḥ khyātir asūyata |**  
**śriyaṁ ca devadevasya patnī nārāyaṇasya yā ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śrīḥ nārāyaṇasya patnī yā tāṁ śriyaṁ cāsūyata ||13||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** evam iti || satīṁ-satīnāmnīm ||11-13|| 

**maitreya uvāca—**  
**kṣīrābdhau śrīḥ samutpannā śrūyate’mṛta-manthane |**  
**bhṛgoḥ khyātyāṁ samutpannety etad āha kathaṁ bhavān ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: praśnaḥ spaṣṭārthaḥ ||14||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** maitreyaścodayati-kṣīrābdhāviti ||14||

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**nityaiva sā jagan-mātā viṣṇoḥ śrīr anapāyinī |**  
**yathā sarva-gato viṣṇus tathaiveyaṁ dvijottama ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uttarasyāyaṁ bhāvaḥ—tasyā utpattimattve bhaved ayaṁ virodhaḥ | nityāyā eva sarva-gatāyāḥ sarvātmikāyāś ca viṣṇu-śaktes tasyāḥ kārya-vaśena viṣṇor ivāvirbhāva-mātram | ataḥ pūrvaṁ bhṛgu-sutā-rūpeṇa āvirbhūtāyā durvāsaḥ-śāpena ca tirobhūtāyāḥ punaḥ kṣirābdhāv āvirbhāvo na virudhyata iti | yad etad āha—nityaiva ity-ādinā yāvad uttarādhyāya-samāptiḥ ||15||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** pariharati-nityeti || viṣṇoḥ-jagatpiturviṣṇoranapāyinyeṣā jaganmātṛtvena tadvannityā | tasyāś ca viṣṇorivāvirbhāvatirobhāvau staḥ | sā pūrvaṁ bhṛgoḥ sutātvenāvirbhūtā, paścādindrasya durvāsasaśśāpāttirobhūtvā'mṛtamathane prādurbhūtā | ato na virodhaḥ | yatheti | sarvagato viṣṇuḥ yathā-yatsvabhāvaḥ, iyam api tathā-tatsvabhāveti, viṣṇoḥ sarvagatatvasatyajñānādisvarūpakalyāṇaguṇādīnāmatideśaḥ | athavā bhagavānvibhutvena sarvagataḥ; asyāstacchaktivaśādaṇutve'pi tatratatra saṁdhānātsarvasagatvamuktam | iyaṁ ca sarvagatā ||15||

**artho viṣṇur iyaṁ vāṇī nītir eṣā nayo hariḥ |**  
**bodho viṣṇur iyaṁ buddhir dharmo’sau tat-kriyā tv iyam ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: lakṣmī-nārāyaṇayoḥ sarvātmakatvaṁ tathā tathopāsanārthaṁ prapañcayati—artho viṣṇur ity-ādinā yāvad adhyāya-samāptiḥ | vāṇī arthābhidhāyikā vāk iyaṁ śrīḥ | nītir daṇḍa-nītir eṣā śrīḥ, nayaḥ samādy-upāyaḥ | bodhaḥ ātma-prakāśaḥ, buddhis tad-abhivyañjikā dhī-vṛttiḥ | dharmo’pūrvaṁ, sat-kriyā yāgādiḥ ||16||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tayoḥ sarvātmakatvamanapāyitvaṁ copapādayati-artha iti || arthaḥ-śabdavādhyaḥ nītiḥ-nyāyaśāstram | nayo-nyāyaḥ | buddhiḥ-adhyavasāyātmakamantaḥkaraṇam, tatkāryo niścayo bodhaḥ | satkriyā-yāgādiḥ | dharmaḥ-tadutpādyamadṛṣṭam ||16||

**sraṣṭā viṣṇur iyaṁ sṛṣṭiḥ śrīr bhūmir bhūdharo hariḥ |**  
**santoṣo bhagavān lakṣaṇśarīrīs tuṣṭir maitreya śāśvatī ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: bhūdharo girir bhūpatir vā | yadṛcchā-lābhair alaṁ pratyayaḥ santoṣaḥ | tathā nirvṛtis tuṣṭiḥ ||17||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** sraṣṭeti || alaṁbuddhistuṣṭiḥ | tadabhivyaktaṁ sukhaṁ santoṣaḥ; śāśvatīti lakṣmyā viśeṣaṇam ||17|| 

**icchā śrīr bhagavān kāmo yajño’sau dakṣiṇā tu sā |**  
**ājyāhutir asau devī puroḍāśo janārdanaḥ ||18||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: icchā dhanādi-spṛhā | kāmas tad-bhogābhilāṣaḥ ||18||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** iccheti || icchā-apekṣā; tajjanyo'bhiniveśaḥ kāmaḥ ||18|| 

**patnīśālā mune lakṣmīḥ prāg-vaṁśo madhusūdanaḥ |**  
**citir lakṣmīr harir yūpa idhmā śrīr bhagavān kuśaḥ ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: citir iṣṭikā-cayanām ||19||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** patnīśāleti || idhmā-samit | ārṣatvāt ṭāp ||19|| 

**sāma-svarūpī bhagavān udgītiḥ kamalālayā |**  
**svāhā lakṣmīr jagannātho vāsudevo hutāśanaḥ ||20||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sāma-svarūpī rathantarādi-gāna-rūpaḥ | udgītis tad-gāna-vyāpāraḥ | hutāśano vāsudevaḥ | svāhā tu lakṣmīḥ ||20||

**śaṅkaro bhagavān śaurir bhūtir gaurī dvijottama |**  
**maitreya keśavaḥ sūryas tat-prabhā kamalālayā ||21||**

**viṣṇuḥ pitṛ-gaṇaḥ padmā svadhā śāśvata-tuṣṭidā |**  
**dyauḥ śrīḥ sarvātmako viṣṇur avakāśo’tivistaraḥ ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dyauḥ śrīḥ | avakāśo viṣṇuḥ ||22||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** sāmasvarūpīti || sagāno maṁtraḥ sāma, tadgānaviśeṣa udgītiḥ ||21-22||

**śaśāṅkaḥ śrīdharaḥ kāntiḥ śrīs tasthaivānapāyinī |**  
**dhṛtir lakṣmīr jagac-ceṣṭā vāyuḥ sarvatrago hariḥ ||23||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dhṛtir medhādi-dhāraṇam, jagac-ceṣṭā ca lakṣmīḥ | tat-kartā vāyur hariḥ ||23||

**jaladhir dvija govindas tad-velā śrīr mahāmate |**  
**lakṣmī-svarūpam indrāṇī devendro madhusūdanaḥ ||24||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** śaśāṅka iti ||vāyuḥ-jagatprāṇaḥ, dhṛtiḥ-dhāraṇaṁ, jagacceṣṭā ca pravahādiprāṇādirūpavāyukṛtyam ||25-26|| 

**yamaś cakradharaḥ sākṣād dhūmorṇā kamalālayā |**  
**ṛddhiḥ śrīḥ śrīdharo devaḥ svayam eva dhaneśvaraḥ ||25||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: dhūmorṇā yamasya bhāryā | dhaneśvaraḥ kuveraḥ | ṛddhis tasya patnī ||25||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** yama iti || yamasya patnī dhūmorṇā | ṛddhiḥ kuberasya ||25|| 

**gaurī lakṣmīr mahābhāgā keśavo varuṇaḥ svayam |**   
**śrīr devasenā viprendra devasenāpatir hariḥ ||26||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: varuṇasya bhāryāpi gaurī-saṁjñā ||26||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** gaurīti || gaurī-varuṇasya patnī | devasenā-skandabhāryā ||26|| 

**avaṣṭambho gadāpāṇiḥ śaktir lakṣmīr dvijottama |**  
**kāṣṭhā lakṣmīr nimeṣo’sau muhūrto’sau kalā tu sā ||27||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: avaṣṭambhaḥ puruṣakāraḥ | śaktis tat-sāmarthyam ||27||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** avaṣṭambha iti || avaṣṭaṁbhaḥ-ādhāro balaṁ vā ||27|| 

**jyotsnā lakṣmīḥ pradīpo’sau sarvaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ |**  
**latā-bhūtā jaganmātā śrīr viṣṇur druma-saṁsthitaḥ ||28||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: jyotsnā prabhā, dīpo hariḥ | harer viśeṣaṇaṁ sarvaḥ sarveśvaraś ceti | druma-rūpaḥ saṁsthito latāyā āśrayaḥ ||28||

**vibhāvarī śrīr divaso devaś cakra-gadādharaḥ |**  
**vara-prado varo viṣṇur vadhūḥ padmavanālayā ||29||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vadhūr jāyā | varaḥ patiḥ ||29||

**nava-svarūpī bhagavān śrīr nadī-rūpa-saṁsthitiḥ |**  
**dhvajaś ca puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ patākā kamalālayā ||30||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** jyotsneti || jyotsnā-prabhā ||28-30||

**tṛṣṇā lakṣmīr jagat-svāmī lobho nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ |**  
**rati-rāgau ca dharmajña lakṣmī-govinda eva ca ||31||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: itas tataḥ punar upāditsā tṛṣṇā, tat-prāpyathārtha-paryāptir lobhaḥ | rāgaḥ kāmaḥ | ratis tat-patnī ||31||

**kiṁ cātibahunoktena saṁkṣepeṇedam ucyate |**  
**deva-tiryaṅ-manuṣyādau puṁ-nāmni bhagavān hariḥ |**  
**strī-nāmni lakṣmīr maitreya nānayor vidyate param ||32||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: anayor ābhyām param anyan na vidyate ||32||

iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśābhidhāyāṁ viṣṇu-purāṇa \-ṭīkāyāṁ prathamāṁśe aṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ |

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tṛṣṇeti || deyasyāditsā niṣiddhalipsā ca lobhaḥ | labdhe'paryāptadhīstṛṣṇā | ratiḥ-priyasaṁgamajā tatkālaprītiḥ | tatprakarṣo rāgaḥ ||

deveti || anayoḥ-ābhyāṁ param-anyat | sarvasyobhayātmakatve'pi tatratatrābhimukhyātiśayaviśeṣāt arthavāṇyādīnāṁ tadātmakatvamuktam ||31-32||

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇavyākhyāne viṣṇucittīye prathame'ṁśe'ṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ ||8||

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe prathame’ṁśe aṣṭamo’dhyāyaḥ   
||8||

—o)0(o—

(1.9)



## **indraṁ prati durvāsasaḥ śāpaḥ, brahmaṇaḥ samīpe devānāṁ gamanaṁ, samudra-manthanaṁ, indrasya lakṣmī-stutiś ca** 

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**idaṁ ca śṛṇu maitreya yat pṛṣṭo’ham iha tvayā |**  
**śrī-sambaddhaṁ mayā hy etac chrutam āsīn marīcitaḥ ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tad evaṁ maitreyakṛtākṣepaparihārārthaṁ sarvātmatvaprapañcanena viṣṇoriva lakṣmyā api nityatvamuktam, idānīm āvirbhāvatirobhāvābhyāṁ taduktaṁ virodhaṁ parihartumāha idañcety ādināpūrvaṁ bhṛgusutā satītyantena granthena | bhṛgusutāpi śrīryathā kṣīrābdhau jātā ity ucyate idañca śṛṇu | mayāpi evam eva sandihānena marīceḥ sakāśād etac śrutamāsīt ||1||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** idam iti || marīciḥ-kāśyapapitā ||1|| 

**durvāsāḥ śaṅkarasyāṁśaś cacāra pṛthivīm imām |**  
**sa dadarśa srajaṁ dviyām ṛṣir vidyādharī-kare ||2||**

**santānakānām akhilaṁ yasyā gandhena vāsitam |**  
**atisevyam abhūd brahman tad-vanaṁ vana-cāriṇām ||3||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tatra prathamaṁ bhṛgusutāyāḥ satyāstirodhāne kāraṇaṁ vaktum āha—unmattavratadhṛgyogino hi jaḍonmattapiśācā iva durvāsā iti | śaṅkarasyāṁśa ity anena tasya śakraśāpasāmarthyam aparādhāsahiṣṇutvañcoktam | santāno devataruḥ, tadīyānāṁ puṣpāṇāṁ srajaṁ mālām | yasyā gandhena vāsitaṁ tad vanaṁ vanacāriṇām atisevyamabhūt ||2-3|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** durvāsā iti || śaṁkarasyāṁśa iti vakṣyamāṇākṣāntyārdehetunirdeśaḥ ||2-3||

**unmatta-vrata-dhṛg vipras tāṁ dṛṣṭvā śobhanāṁ srajam |**  
**tāṁ yayāce varārohāṁ vidyādhara-vadhūṁ tataḥ ||4||**

**yācitā tena tanvaṅgī mālāṁ vidyādharāṅganā |**  
**dadau tasmai viśālākṣī sādaraṁ praṇipatya ca ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vartante | tāṁ srajaṁ tāṁ vidyādharavadhūṁ yācitavān iti dvikarmako yācati ||4-5||

**tām ādāyātmano mūrdhni srajam unmatta-rūpa-dhṛk |**  
**kṛtvā sa vipro maitreya paribabhrāma medinīm ||6||**

**sa dadarśa samāyāntam unmattairāvatā-sthitam |**  
**trailokyādhipatiṁ devaṁ saha devaiḥ śacī-patim ||7||**

**tām ātmanaḥ sa śirasaḥ srajam unmatta-ṣaṭpadām |**  
**ādāyāmara-rājāya cikṣeponmattavan muniḥ ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tāṁ srajaṁ mūrdhni kṛtvā medinīṁ parivabhrāma ity anvayaḥ ||6-8|| 

**gṛhītvāmara-rājena srag airāvata-mūrdhani |**  
**nyastā rarāja kailāsa-śikhare jāhnavī yathā ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: airāvatamūrddhani nyastā sā ca kailāsaśikhare jāhnavī iva rarāja ||9|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** unmatteti || unmattavratadhṛk | yogino hi jaḍonmattapiśācavadvartante | athavā sanatkumāraśāpādunmattavṛttadhṛk ||4-9||

**madāndhakāritākṣo’sau gandhākṛṣṭena vāraṇaḥ |**  
**kareṇāghrāya cikṣepa tāṁ srajaṁ dharaṇī-tale ||10||**

**tataś cukrodha bhagavān durvāsā muni-sattamaḥ |**  
**maitreya deva-rājaṁ taṁ kruddhaś caitad uvāca ha ||11||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: madena andhakārite sañjātāndhakāre akṣiṇī yasya asau | kareṇa āghrāya iti-kāraṇaḥ karasyaiva ghrāṇatvāt ||10-11||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** madāndheti || gandhākṛṣṭeneti pāṭhāntaram | kāraṇāṁ karasya gaṁdhākṛṣṭhatvaṁ tasyaiva nāsātvāt ||10-11||

**aiśvarya-matta duṣtātmann atistabdho’si vāsava |**  
**śriyo dhāma srajaṁ yas tvaṁ mad-dattāṁ nābhinandasi ||12||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atistabdho'si garvitā'si | śriyo dhāma lakṣyā nivāsabhūtām ||12|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** aiśvaryeti || stabdhaḥ-avinayoddhataḥ | atra hetuḥ śriyeti | śriyo dhāmeti vā pāṭhaḥ ||12|| 

**prasāda iti noktaṁ te praṇipāda-puraḥsaram |**  
**harṣotphulla-kapolena na cāpi śirasā dhṛtā ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: te tvayā harṣeṇa utphullau vikasitau kapolau yasya tathābhūtena satā tvayā ||13|| 

**mayā dattām imāṁ mālāṁ yasmān na bahu manyase |**  
**trailokya-śrīr ato mūḍha vināśam upayāsyati ||14||**

**māṁ manyate’nyaiḥ sadṛśaṁ nyūnaṁ śakra bhavān dvijaiḥ |**  
**ato’vamānam asmākaṁ māninā bhavatā kṛtam ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: trailokyaśrīstava trailokyaiśvaryyam vināśam, ato mālābahumānākaraṇadoṣāt ||14-15||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** prasāda iti || te-svayā ||13-15|| 

**mad-dattā bhavatā yasmāt kṣiptā mālā mahī-tale |**  
**tasmāt praṇaṣṭa-lakṣmīkaṁ trailokyaṁ te bhaviṣyati ||16||**

**yasya sañjāta-kopasya bhayam eti carācaram |**  
**taṁ tvaṁ mām atigarveṇa devarājāvamanyase ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: gajena kṣiptāyā upekṣitatvād bhavataiva kṣiptā ity uktam tasmānmālāyā dharaṇītale prakṣepadoṣāt | tvadīyaṁ trailokyaṁ pranaṣṭalakṣmīkaṁ dāridryābhibhūtaṁ bhaviṣyati iti dvitīyaḥ śāpaḥ ||16-17|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** mahatteti || pranaṣṭalakṣmīkaṁ-tirohitalakṣmīkam | atra pranaṣṭaśabdasya tirohitatvamarthaḥ ||16-17|| 

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**mahendro vāraṇaskāndhād avatīrya tvarānvitaḥ |**  
**prasādayāmāsa tadā durvāsasam akalmaṣam ||18||**

**prasādyamānaḥ sa tadā praṇipāta-puraḥsaram |**  
**pratyuvāca sahasrākṣaṁ durvāsā muni-sattama ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: akalmaṣaṁ sāparādhaśāpe doṣobhāvāt ||18-19|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** mahendra iti || akalmaṣaṁ-sāparādhaśāpe doṣābhāvāt ||18-19||

**durvāsā uvāca—**  
**nāhaṁ kṛpālu-hṛdayo na ca māṁ bhajate kṣamā |**  
**anye te munayaḥ śakra durvāsasam avehi mām ||20||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: anye te munayaḥ ye dayālavaḥ | ahaṁ tu na tathā ||20||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** nāham iti || anye te munayaḥ, ye kṣamāvantaḥ ||20||

**gautamādibhir anyais tvaṁ garvam āpādito mudhā |**   
**akṣānti-sāra-sarvasvaṁ durvāsasam avehi mām ||21||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tadevāha, gautamādibhiḥ svabhāryādharṣaṇādyaparādhe'pi tvayi dākṣiṇyena anugrahaparaiḥ mudhā vṛthaiva garvaṁ prāpito'si | akṣāntau eva sārastapobalaṁ, tad eva sarvasvaṁ yasya taṁ mām ||21||

**vasiṣṭhādyair dayā-sāraiḥ stotraṁ kurvadbhir uccakaiḥ |**  
**garvaṁ gato’si uyenaivaṁ mām apy adyāvamanyase ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uccair uccakaiḥ stuvadbhiḥ | yad vā, uccakair unnamitaiḥ śirobhir uccāsanopaviṣṭasya evaṁ stotraṁ kurvadbhir ity arthaḥ ||22||

**jvalaj-jaṭā-kalāpasya bhṛkuṭī-kuṭilaṁ mukham |**  
**nirīkṣya kas tribhuvane mama yo na gato bhayam ||23||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: evaṁ sati | jvalaj-jaṭeti | mama mukhaṁ nirīkṣya yo bhayaṁ na gataḥ, sa kaḥ ? na ko’pīty arthaḥ ||23||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** gautamādibhiriti || gautamo hi ahalyādharṣakaṁ tvāṁ sarvāṅgabhago bhaveti śaptvā punastvatprasāditaḥ sarvāṅganetraṁ cakre | akṣāntisārasarvasvam-naivaṁ kāruṇiko'ham iti bhāvaḥ ||21-23||

**viḍambanām iyāṁ bhūyaḥ karoṣy anunayātmikām ||24||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: viḍambanām avahāsam ||24||

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**ity uktvā prayayau vipro devarājo’pi taṁ punaḥ |**  
**āruhyairāvataṁ brahman prayaāv amarāvatīm ||25||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** nāham iti || viḍambanā-avamānaḥ ||24-25||

**tataḥ prabhṛti niḥśaktaṁ sa-śakraṁ bhuvana-trayam |**  
**maitreyāsīd apadhvastaṁ saṅkṣīṇauṣadhi-vīrudham ||26||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: apadhvastaṁ naṣṭaprāyam ||26|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ**: tata iti || niśśrīkatvaṁ--bhogya-vastv-abhāva eva | evam auṣadhy-ādi-bhogyābhāvaṁ tat-sādhana-yajña-sattvādy-abhāvaṁ cāha—saṁkṣīṇety-ādinā ||26–28||

**na yajñāḥ sampravartante na tapasyanti tāpasāḥ |**  
**na ca dānādi-dharmeṣu manaś cakre tadā janaḥ ||27||**  
**niḥsattvāḥ sakalā lokā lobhādy-upahatendriyāḥ |**  
**svalpe’pi hi babhūvus te sābhilāṣā dvijottama ||28||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: niḥsattvāḥ dhairya-śūnyāḥ |  ato lobhādibhiḥ upahatendriyāḥ | ataḥ svalpe'py arthe sābhilāṣāḥ ||28||

**yataḥ sattvaṁ tato lakṣmīḥ sattvaṁ bhūty-anusāri ca |**  
**niḥśrīkāṇāṁ kutaḥ sattvaṁ vinā tena guṇāḥ kutaḥ ||29||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: etad eva spaṣṭayati—yata iti | yato yatra sattvaṁ dhairyaṁ, tatra lakṣmīḥ | sattvaṁ bhūty-anusāri, lakṣmyā evānusāri, lakṣmyā evānuvarti | evaṁ dhairya-lakṣmyoḥ parasparāvinābhūtatvāt, śrī-nivṛttyā sattva-nivṛttim āha—niḥśrīkāṇām iti | tena sattvena vinā guṇā audārya-santoṣa-kṣamā-śīlādayaḥ kutaḥ ? ||29|| 

**bala-śauryādy-abhāvaś ca puruṣāṇāṁ guṇair vinā |**  
**laṅghanīyaḥ samastasya bala-śaurya-vivarjitaḥ ||30||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tato'narthaparamparāmāha baleti | laṅghanīyaḥ abhibhāvyaḥ ||30|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** yata iti || sattvaṁ-dhairyam, sattvaguṇo vā | bhūtirlakṣmīḥ | sattvatbhūyoritaretarahetutvam | guṇāḥ—satyaśaucaśīlādyāḥ ||29-30||

**bhavaty apadhvasta-matir laṅghitaḥ prathitaḥ pumān ||31||**

**evam atyanta-niḥśakte trailokye sattva-varjite |**  
**devān prati balodyogaṁ cakrur daiteya-dānavāḥ ||32||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: prathitaḥ prakhyātaḥ pumān laṅghitaḥ avajñātaḥ san apadhvastamatiḥ naṣṭaprajño bhavati ||31-32||

**lobhābhibhūtā niḥśaktā daityāḥ sattva-vivarjitāḥ |**  
**śriyā vihīnair niḥsattvair devaiś cakrus tato raṇam ||33||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** bhavatīti || prathitaḥ-prasiddhaḥ pumān laṁghitaḥ-avajñātaḥ pumān apadhvastamatirbhavati ||31-33||

**vijitās tridaśā daityair indrādyāḥ śaraṇaṁ yayuḥ |**  
**pitāmahaṁ mahā-bhāgaṁ hutāśana-purogamāḥ ||34||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: raṇa yuddhaṁ indrāparādhena trailokyasya niḥśrīkatvaṁ prāptam atastrailokyāntavartitayā prāpnu vadati tadvipakṣeṣu daiteṣu deveṣu iva nātiprabhūtam iti daityānāṁ jayaḥ saṅgacchate ||

 hutāśanapurogamā iti agnerdūtattvāt purogamatvam agnirdevānāṁ dūta āsīd iti śruteḥ ||34||

**yathāvat kathito devair brahmā prāha tataḥ surān |**  
**parāvareśaṁ śaraṇaṁ vrajadhvam asurārdanam ||35||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** vijitā iti || niśśrīkatvādidoṣasāmye'pi guṇitvāprakṛticyutā devā nirguṇatvaprakṛtisthitairdaityarnirjitāḥ ||34-35||

**utpatti-sthiti-nāśānām ahetuṁ hetum īśvaram |**  
**prajāpati-patiṁ viṣṇum anantam aparājitam ||36||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: jagadutpattyādīnāṁ hetum | svayam ahetum svata eva nityasiddham ||36||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** utpattīti || ahetuṁ-svayaṁ heturahitam na cāsya kaścijjanitā ity-ādiśruteḥ | hetuṁ sarvasyotpattyādeḥ ||36||

**pradhāna-puṁsor ajayoḥ kāraṇa-kārya-bhūtayoḥ |**  
**praṇatārti-haraṁ viṣṇuṁ sa vaḥ śreyo vidhāsyati ||37||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ajayoḥ kāryabhūtayor iti janmarahitayor api tayoḥ sargābhimukhīkaraṇena kāryatvam ||37|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** pradhāneti || ajayor api kāryatvaṁ vikāryatvāt svarūpasvabhāvānyathābhāvena ca ||37|| 

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**evam uktvā surān sarvān brahmā loka-pitāmahaḥ |**  
**kṣīrodasyottaraṁ tīraṁ tair eva sahito yayau ||38||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: uttaradigavasthitaṁ tīraṁ paraṁ kūlam iti vā ||38||

**sa gatvā tridaśaiḥ sarvaiḥ samavetaḥ pitāmahaḥ |**  
**tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ parāvara-patiṁ harim ||39||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: iṣṭābhiḥ pūjitābhiḥ apekṣitārthadyotikābhiriti vā parāparāṇām utkṛṣṭanikṛṣṭānāṁ sarvajīvānāṁ patim ||39||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** evam iti || uttaraṁ tīram-uttaraṁ kūlaṁ śākadvīpāśritam ||38-39|| 

**brahmovāca—**  
**namāma[^3] sarvaṁ sarveśam anantam ajam avyayam |**  
**loka-dhāma-dharādhāram aprakāśam abhedinam ||39||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: namāma ity uttara-śloke’pi sambandhaḥ | sarvaṁ sarva-svarūpaṁ sarvasyeśvaraṁ ca | loke ye dhāma-dharāḥ prabhāvavantas teṣām ādhāram | indrādīnāṁ prabhāvo yad-āśraya ity arthaḥ | abhedinaṁ nirbhedaṁ, aprakāśaṁ sva-vyatirikta-prakāśa-śūnyam ity arthaḥ ||39||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** namāmīti || avyayam-apakṣayādivikārarahitan | abhedine-bhedānarham ||39|| 

**nārāyaṇa-maṇīyāṁsam aśeṣāṇām aṇīyasām |**  
**samastānāṁ gariṣṭhaṁ yad bhūr-ādīnāṁ garīyasām ||40||**

**yatra sarvaṁ yataḥ sarvam utpannaṁ sat-puraḥsaram |**  
**sarva-bhūtaś ca yo devaḥ parāṇām api yaḥ paraḥ ||41||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yatra sarvam ity-ādi yat śabdānāṁ sa ādyaḥ pumān prasīdatu iti tṛtīyena anvayaḥ | parāṇām arthādīnām api yaḥ paraḥ puruṣaḥ, tathā ca śrutiḥ—

indriyebhyaḥ parā hy arthā arthebhyaś ca paraṁ manaḥ |  
manasas tu parā buddhir buddher ātmā mahān paraḥ |  
mahataḥ param avyaktam avyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥ || iti ||41||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** nārāyaṇam iti || aṇīyasām-ātmanām ||40-41|| 

**paraḥ parasmāt puruṣāt paramātma-svarūpa-dhṛk |**  
**yogibhiś cintyate yo’sau mukti-hetur mumukṣubhiḥ ||42||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasmāt parasmāt avyakta-prerakāt kāraṇātmanaḥ puruṣād api yaḥ paramātmaiva svarūpa-dhṛk mūrti-dhārī, ata eva yogibhiś cintyate yo’sau ||42||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** para iti | parasmāt-muktāt ||42|| 

**sattvādayo na santīśe yatra ca prākṛtā guṇāḥ |**  
**sa śuddhaḥ sarva-śuddhebhyaḥ pumān ādyaḥ prasīdatu ||43||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** sattvādaya iti | ataḥ sarvabhūtebhyaḥ śuddhaḥ ||43||

**kalā-kāṣṭhā-nimeṣādi-kāla-sūtrasya gocare |**  
**yasya śaktir na śuddhasya prasīdatu sa me hariḥ ||44||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kalā-kāṣṭhā-nimeṣādi-kāla eva sūtravat sūtraṁ jagac-ceṣṭā niyāmakatvāt tasya gocare viṣaye yasya śaktir lakṣmīr na vartate | svarūpābhinnatvān nityaiva sā kālādhīnā na bhavatīty arthaḥ | ata eva tasyāḥ svarūpābhedāc chuddhasyety uktam ||44||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** kaleti || śaktiḥ-lakṣmīḥ | vigrahaparijanaparicchadādivirbhūtiḥ | kalāmuhūrtādimayaś ca kālo na dvibhūteḥ pariṇāmahetuḥ ity-ādeḥ ||44||

**procyate parameśo yo yaḥ śuddho’py upacārataḥ |**  
**prasīdatu sa no viṣṇur ātmā yaḥ sarva-dehinām ||45||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: nanu yadi lakṣmīs tat-svarūpābhinnā kathaṁ tarhi lakṣmyāḥ patir ucyate? tatrāha—procyate iti | parā cāsau mā ca lakṣmīḥ, tasyā īśaḥ parameśo yaḥ śuddhaḥ kevalo’pi upacārato bheda-vivakṣayā procyate | dvitīyo yac-chabdaḥ prasiddhau ||45||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** procyata iti || upacārataḥ | śuddhaḥ-muktaḥ, pūrvamavidyāntargatatvena śuddhyabhāvāt yaḥ śuddho'pyu cārata ity anvayaḥ | atra hetuḥ ātmā yassarvadehinām iti ||46|| 

**yaḥ kāraṇaṁ ca kāryaṁ ca kāraṇasyāpi kāraṇam |**  
**kāryasyāpi ca yaḥ kāryaṁ prasīdatu sa no hariḥ ||46||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** ya iti || kāraṇam iti || kāraṇa-prakṛtiḥ mahataḥ kāraṇatvāt, kāryaṁ-mahān | kāraṇasya-prakṛterapi kāraṇaṁ brahma | kāryasya-mahataḥ kāryamahaṁkāraḥ ||46||

**kārya-kāryasya yat kāryaṁ yat kāryasyāpi yaḥ svayam |**  
**tat-kārya-kārya-bhūto yas tataś ca praṇatāḥ sma tam ||48||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pūrvaślokārthaṁ prapañcayati kāryakāryasyeti dvābhyām | prakṛtikāryasya mahato yat kāryamahaṅkārākhyaṁ, tasya kāryaṁ bhūtasūkṣmavargaḥ | tasyāpi kāryaṁ bhūtabhūtavargaḥ | tatkāryaṁ brahmāṇḍam | tasya kāryabhūto brahmadakṣādivargaḥ, tataś ca tat putrapautrapravāhabhūto yaḥ svayameva, taṁ praṇatāḥ ity anvayaḥ ||48||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** kāryakāryasyeti || kāryakāryasya-kāryabhūtamahatkāryasya ahaṁkārasya kāryaṁ tanmātrāpaścakaṁ, tasyāpi kāryaṁ bhūtapañcakaṁ, tatkāryasyāṇḍasya kāryaṁ caturmukhaḥ, tataś ca kāryam ity anuṣaṅgaḥ, tatkāryaṁ jagat | tatsarvaṁ yaḥ svayameṣa, taṁ praṇatāsmetyanvayaḥ ||48||

**kāraṇaṁ kāraṇasyāpi tasya kāraṇa-kāraṇam |**  
**tat-kāraṇānāṁ hetuṁ taṁ praṇatāḥ sma pareśvaram ||49||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** kāraṇam iti || kāraṇasya-jagatkāraṇasya caturmukhasya, kāraṇamaṇḍaṁ, tasya kāraṇaṁ bhūtapaṁcakaṁ, tatkāraṇaṁ tanmātrāpañcakaṁ, tākāraṇānām-ahaṁkāramahatprakṛtīnāṁ hetuṁ-kāraṇam | kāraṇāvasthaṁ kāryāvasthaṁ ca sarvaṁ (sva) tvamevety arthaḥ ||49||

**bhoktāraṁ bhogya-bhūtaṁ ca sraṣṭāraṁ sṛjyam eva ca |**  
**kārya-kartṛ-svarūpaṁ taṁ praṇatāḥ sma paraṁ padam ||50||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tathā kāraṇam arvāksṛṣṭirbrahmādi, tasya kāraṇaṁ brahmāṇḍam, tasya kāraṇam mahābhūtāni, tatkāraṇaṁ bhūtasūkṣmāṇi, tatkāraṇānām ahaṅkāramahatsūtrāṇāṁ hetuṁ pradhānabhūtaṁ praṇatāḥ sma ity arthaḥ | prakṛterguṇakṣobhāt prathamaṁ kriyāśaktisūtram utpadyate | tato jñānaśakti mahattattvaṁ tato'haṅkāra iti prakriyāyāṁ tatkāraṇānām ity anena bahuvacanāntena ahaṅkāramahatsūtrāṇāṁ grahaṇam | taduktaṁ sattvaṁ rajastama iti trivṛdekamādau sūtraṁ mahānaham iti pravadanti jīvam | iti yadvā prakṛtyā saha tatkāraṇānām iti bahutvasampādya taddhetuṁ prakṛtiprerakam īśvaraṁ praṇatāḥ sma iti yojanīyam ||49-50||

**viśuddha-bodhavan nityam ajam akṣayam avyayam |**  
**avyaktam avikāraṁ yat tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṁ padam ||51||**

**na sthūlaṁ na ca sūkṣmaṁ yan na viśeṣaṇāgocaram |**  
**tat padaṁ paramaṁ viṣṇoḥ praṇamāmaḥ sadāmalam ||52||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: viśuddhaṁ bodhanaṁ śuddhaṁ jñānaṁ vṛttijñānaṁ vyāvartayan śuddhatvaṁ darśayati, avyaktaṁ vyaktaṁ viṣayaḥ tad rahitam adhikārañceti | tadupapādayati, nityam ity-ādinā | akṣayamanādhāraṁ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṁ padaṁ praṇamāma ityuttareṇa anvayaḥ ||51-52||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** bhoktāram iti || bhojyaṁ-bhogyaṁ śabdādi, sṛjyaṁ--ghaṭādi, kāryaṁ-yāgādi gatyādi ca | paraṁ padaṁ-paramaṁ prāpyasthānam ||50-52|| 

**yasyāyutāyutāṁśāṁśe viśva-śaktir iyaṁ sthitā |**  
**para-brahma-svarūpaṁ yat praṇamāmas tam avyayam ||53||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** yasyeti || ayutāṁśo yaḥ, tasyāyutāṁśo yaḥ, tasyāṁśe sthitā merorivāṇuḥ pādo'syetyādiḥ viśvaśaktiḥ jaganmayī ||53|| 

**yad yoginaḥ sadodyuktāḥ puṇya-pāpa-kṣaye’kṣayam |**  
**paśyanti praṇave cintyaṁ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṁ padam ||54||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yasya acintyānantaśakterayutāṁśāṁśo māyāśaktileśaḥ tasyāṁśo rajoguṇastasmin iyaṁ viśvaracanāśaktiḥ sthitā, taṁ praṇamāma ityasya uttaraślokatraye'pi anuṣaṅgaḥ ||53-54|| 

**yan na devā na munayo na cāhaṁ na ca śaṅkaraḥ |**  
**jānanti parammeśasya tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṁ padam ||55||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: puṇyapāpakṣaye tatpratibandhāpagame praṇave sthitaṁ mahāvākyārthaviṣayatvāt tasya ||55||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** yaditi || akṣayam iti padacchedaḥ ||54-55||

**śaktayo yasya devasya brahma-viṣṇu-śivātmikāḥ |**  
**bhavanty abhūta-pūrvasya tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṁ padam ||56||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: abhūtapūrvasya na bhūtaḥ kaścidati pūrvo yasmāt, anāderity arthaḥ | yasminnajātaḥ paro'nyo'sti ya āviveśa bhuvanāni viśvāḥ iti śruteḥ ||56||

**sarveśa sarva-bhūtātman sarva sarvāśrayācyuta |**  
**prasīda viṣṇo bhaktānāṁ vraja no dṛṣṭi-gocaram ||57||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tad evaṁ stutvā prārthayate sarveśeti ||56-57|| 

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**ity udīritam ākarṇya brahmaṇas tridaśās tataḥ |**  
**praṇamyocuḥ prasīdeti vraja no dṛṣṭi-gocaram ||58||**

**yan nāyaṁ bhagavān brahmā jānāti paramaṁ padam |**  
**tan-natāḥ sma jagad-dhāma tava sarva-gatācyuta ||59||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: jagaddhāma jagataḥ prakāśakam āśrayabhūtam iti vā ||59||

**ity ante vacasas teṣāṁ devānāṁ brahmaṇas tathā |**  
**ūcur devarṣayaḥ sarve bṛhaspati-purogamāḥ ||60||**

**ādyo yajña-pumān īḍyaḥ pūrveṣāṁ yaś ca pūrvajaḥ |**  
**tan-natāḥ sma jagat-sraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭāram aviśeṣaṇam ||61||**

**bhagavan bhūta-bhavyeśa yajña-mūrti-dharāvyaya |**  
**prasīda praṇatānāṁ tvaṁ sarveṣāṁ dehi darśanam ||62||**

**eṣa brahmā sahāsmābhiḥ saha-rudrais trilocanaḥ |**  
**sarvādityaiḥ samaṁ pūṣā pāvako’yaṁ sahāgnibhiḥ ||63||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: praṇatānāṁ prasīda ity uktvā tānevāhuḥ—eṣa brahmeti tribhiḥ ||63|| 

**aśvinau vasavaś ceme sarve caite marudgaṇāḥ |**  
**sādhyā viśve tathā devā devendraś cāyam īśvaraḥ ||64||**

**praṇāma-pravaṇā nātha daitya-sainyaiḥ parājitāḥ |**  
**śaraṇaṁ tvām anuprāptāḥ samastā devatā-gaṇāḥ ||65||**

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**evaṁ saṁstūyamānas tu bhagavān śaṅkha-cakra-dhṛk |**  
**jagāma darśanaṁ teṣāṁ maitreya parameśvaraḥ ||66||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** abhūtapūrvasya-na bhūtaṁ pūrvaṁ yasmāt tasya; sa hi sarvasmātpūrvaḥ | bhūtapūrvasyeti pāṭhe bhūtānāṁ pūrva iti ||56-66||

**taṁ dṛṣṭvā te tadā devāḥ śaṅkha-cakra-gadādharam |**  
**apūrva-rūpa-saṁsthānaṁ tejasāṁ rāśi-mūrtijam ||67||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: apūrvaṁ rūpasaṁsthānaṁ daihikaḥ sanniveśo yasya tam ||67|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tam iti || apūrvarūpasaṁsthānaṁ-samastalokavilakṣaṇavarṇāṅgasanniveśam ||67|| 

**praṇamya praṇatāḥ sarve saṅkṣobha-stimitekṣaṇāḥ |**  
**tuṣṭuvuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṁ pitāmaha-purogamāḥ ||68||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pūrvaṁ praṇatā api bhaktyā punaḥ praṇamya tuṣṭuvuḥ ||68||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** praṇamyeti || praṇamya praṇatāḥ-pūrvaṁ praṇatā api bhaktyā punaḥ praṇamya ||68|| 

**devā ūcuḥ—**  
**namo namo’viśeṣas tvaṁ tvaṁ brahmā tvaṁ pināka-dhṛk |**  
**indras tvam agniḥ pavano varuṇaḥ savitā yamaḥ ||69||**

**vasavo marutaḥ sādhyā viśvedeva-gaṇāḥ bhavān |**  
**yo’yaṁ tavāgrato deva samīpaṁ devatā-gaṇaḥ |**  
**sa tvam eva jagat-sraṣṭā yataḥ sarva-gato bhavān ||70||**

**tvaṁ yajñas tvaṁ vaṣāṭ-kāras tvam oṁkāraḥ prajāpatiḥ |**  
**vidyā vedyaṁ ca sarvātmaṁs tvan-mayaṁ cākhilaṁ jagat ||71||**

**tvām ārtāḥ śaraṇaṁ viṣṇo prayātā daitya-nirjitāḥ |**  
**vayaṁ prasīda sarvātmaṁs tejasāpyāyayasva naḥ ||72||**

**tāvad ārtis tathā vāñchā tāvan mohas tathāsukham |**  
**yāvan na yāti śaraṇaṁ tvām aśeṣādhanāśanam ||73||**

**tvaṁ prasādaṁ prasannātman prapannānāṁ kuruṣva naḥ |**  
**tejasāṁ nātha sarveṣāṁ sva-śaktyāpyāyanaṁ kuru ||74||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tejasā prabhāvadinā no'smān apyāyayasva saṁvardhaya | ārtiḥ śatrupīḍā, asukhaṁ duḥkham || svaśaktyā lakṣmyā ||74||  
| 

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**evaṁ saṁstūyamānas tu praṇatair amarair hariḥ |**  
**prasanna-dṛṣṭir bhagavān idam āha sa viśvakṛt ||75||**

**tejaso bhavatāṁ devāḥ kariṣyāmy upabṛṁhaṇam |**  
**vadāmy ahaṁ yat kriyatāṁ bhavadbhis tad idaṁ surāḥ ||76||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: bhagavān idamāha ity-āderbhāgavatokto'bhiprāyaḥ | taduktam 

eka eveśvarastasmin surakārye sureśvaraḥ |   
vihartukāmastānāha samudronmathanādibhiḥ iti ||75-76|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** namonama iti || aviśeṣaḥ-sarvasamaḥ ||69-76|| 

**ānīya sahitā daityaiḥ kṣirābdhau sakalauṣadhīḥ |**  
**prakṣipyātrāmṛtārthaṁ tāḥ sakalā daitya-dānavaiḥ |**  
**manthānaṁ mandaraṁ kṛtvā netraṁ kṛtvā ca vāsukim ||77||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kṣīrābdhau kṣiptveti śeṣaḥ | netraṁ manthanarajjum ||77||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** ānīyeti || oṣadhīnāṁ vicitraśaktikavādvicitravastūtpatty arthamānayanam ||77|| 

**mathyatām amṛtaṁ devāḥ sahāye mayy avasthite ||78||**

**sāma-pūrvaṁ ca daiteyās tatra sāhāyya-karmaṇi |**  
**sāmānya-phala-bhoktāro yūyaṁ vācyā bhaviṣyatha ||79||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: amṛtaṁ mathyatāṁ mathanena amṛtaṁ utpādyatām ity arthaḥ || sāmapūrvam upapattipūrvakaṁ sāmānyaṁ yat phalaṁ bhoktāro yūyañca bhaviṣyatha iti vācyāḥ ||79||  
||

**mathyamāne ca tatrābdhau yat samutpatsyate’mṛtam |**  
**tat-pānād balino yūyam amarāś ca bhaviṣyatha ||80||**

**tathā cāhaṁ kariṣyāmi te yathā tridaśa-dviṣaḥ |**  
**na prāpsyanty amṛtaṁ devāḥ kevalaṁ kleśa-bhāginaḥ ||81||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tarhi te'pi tathā bhaviṣyantīti śaṅkamānān pratyāha—tathā ceti | bho devāḥ | te yuṣmadviṣaḥ kevalaṁ kleśabhāgino yathā bhaviṣyanti, tathā kariṣyāmi ||81||

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**ity uktvā devadevena sarva eva tataḥ surāḥ |**  
**sandhānam asuraiḥ kṛtvā yatnavanto’mṛte’bhavan ||82||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: amṛte'mṛtārtham ||82|| 

**nānauṣadhīḥ samānīya deva-daiteya-dānavāḥ |**  
**kṣiptvā kṣīrābdhi-payasi śarada-bhrāmala-tviṣi ||83||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śaradabhrasyeva amalā tviṭ dīptiryasya tasmin ||82|| 

**manthānaṁ mandaraṁ kṛtvā netraṁ kṛtvā ca vāsukim |**  
**tato mathitum ārabdhā maitreya tarasāmṛtam ||84||**

**vibudhāḥ sahitāḥ sarve yataḥ pucchaṁ tataḥ kṛtāḥ |**  
**kṛṣṇena vāsuker daityāḥ pūrvakāye niveśitāḥ ||85||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** madhyatām iti || amṛtaṁ mathyatāṁ-mathanenāmṛtamutpādyatām ||78-85||

**te tasya mukha-niśvāsa-vahni-tāpa-hata-tviṣaḥ |**  
**nistejaso’surāḥ sarve babhūvur amitaujasaḥ ||86||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: amṛtaṁ mathitum ārabdhāḥ | kartari ktaḥ ārabdhavanta ity arthaḥ ||84-86|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** ta iti || amitaujasastasyetyanvayaḥ ||86|| 

**tenaiva mukha-niśvāsa-vāyunāsta-balāhakaiḥ |**  
**puccha-pradeśe varṣadbhis tadā cāpyāyitāḥ surāḥ ||87||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yena asurāṇāṁ duḥsaho vahnirutpāditaḥ | tenaiva vāsukermakhaniḥśvāsavāyunā astabalāhakaiḥ kṣiptairmeghaiḥ ||86||

**kṣīroda-madhye bhagavān kūrma-rūpī svayaṁ hariḥ |**  
**manthanādrer adhiṣṭhānaṁ bhramato’bhūn mahāmune ||88||**

**rūpeṇānyena devānāṁ madhye cakra-gadādharaḥ |**  
**cakarṣa nāgarājānaṁ daitya-madhye’pareṇa ca ||89||**

**uparyākrāntavāñ chailaṁ bṛhad-rūpeṇa keśavaḥ |**  
**tathāpareṇa maitreya yan na dṛṣṭaṁ surāsuraiḥ ||90||**

**tejasā nāgarājānaṁ tathāpyāyitavān hariḥ |**  
**anyena tejasā devānupabṛṁhitavān prabhuḥ ||91||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sahāye mayi avasthita iti yaduktaṁ, tatsāhāyyam āha—kṣīrodamadhya iti caturbhiḥ ||88-91|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tenaiveti || vahniinā'staṁ balāhakairiti pāṭhe, pucche vahninā astaṁ-saṁkṣīṇam ity arthaḥ | balāhakaiḥ-bhagavatā sṛṣtaiḥ ||87-91|| 

**mathyamāne tatas tasmin kṣīrābdhau deva-dānavaiḥ |**  
**havir dhāmābhavat pūrvaṁ surabhiḥ sura-pūjitā ||92||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: haviṣaḥ kṣīradadhyāderdhāma āśrayabhūtā ||92|| 

**jagmur mudaṁ tato devā dānavāś ca mahā-mune |**  
**vyākṣipta-cetasaś caiva babhūvuḥ stimitekṣaṇāḥ ||93||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vyākṣiptacetasaḥ tallobhākṛṣṭamanasaḥ ||93|| 

**kim etad iti siddhānāṁ divi cintayatāṁ tataḥ |**  
**babhūva vāruṇī devī madāghūrṇita-locanā ||94||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vārūṇī madirādhiṣṭhātrī devī ||94|| 

**kṛtāvartāt tatas tasmāt kṣīrodād vāsayañ jagat |**  
**gandhena pārijāto’bhūd deva-strī-nandanas taruḥ ||95||**

**rūpaudārya-guṇopetas tathā cāpsarasāṁ gaṇaḥ |**  
**kṣīrodadheḥ samutpanno maitreya paramādbhutaḥ ||96||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: mandarabhramaṇena kṛtā ambhasām āvartāṁ yasmin tasmāt ||95-96||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** mathyamāna iti || havirddhāma-haviṣa āśrayaḥ ||92-96|| 

**tataḥ śītāṁśur abhavaj jagṛhe taṁ maheśvaraḥ |**  
**jagṛhuś ca viṣaṁ nāgāḥ kṣīrodābdhi-samutthitam ||97||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vipañca maheśvaro jagṛhe | taccheṣañca nāgā jagṛhuḥ | taduktaṁ 

praskannaṁ pibataḥ pāṇeryat kiñcijjagṛhuḥ sma tat |   
vṛścikāhiviṣauṣadhyo dandaśūkāś ca ye pare iti ||97||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tata iti || ādau bhagavanmanaso jātasya caṁdrasya dvau dehau | tatraiko'bdhijaḥ śivaśirobhūṣaṇam; anyastvatrinetrajo lokayātrāniyuktaḥ | nāgāś ceti caśabdānmaheśvaro'pi viṣaṁ jagrāha ||97||

**tato dhanvantarir devaḥ śvetāmbara-dharaḥ svayam |**  
**bibhrat-kamaṇḍaluṁ pūrṇam amṛtasya samutthitaḥ ||98||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: amṛtasya kamaṇḍaluṁ tenaiva pūrṇaṁ vibhrata samutthitaḥ ||98||

**tataḥ svastha-manaskās te sarve daiteya-dānavāḥ |**  
**babhūvur muditāḥ sarve maitreya munibhiḥ saha ||99||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tata iti || amṛtasya pūrṇam iti tṛtīyārthe ṣaṣṭhī ||98-99||

**tataḥ sphurat-kāntimatī vikāsi-kamale sthitā |**  
**śrīr devī payasas tasmād udbhūtā dhṛta-paṅkajā ||100||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: svasthamanaso babhūvuḥ ||99-100|| 

**tāṁ tuṣṭuvur mudā yuktāḥ śrī-sūktena maharṣayaḥ ||101||**

**viśvāvasu-mukhās tasyā gandharvāḥ purato jaguḥ |**  
**ghṛtācī-pramukhās tatra nanṛtuś cāpasaro-gaṇāḥ ||102||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śrīsūktena hiraṇyavarṇām iti pañcadarśarcena ||102|| 

**gaṅgādyāḥ saritas toyaiḥ snānārtham upatasthire |**  
**diggajā hema-pātra-stham ādāya vimalaṁ jalam |**  
**snāpayāñcakrire devīṁ sarva-loka-maheśvarīm ||103||**

**kṣīrodo rūpa-dhṛk tasyai mālām amlāna-paṅkajām |**  
**dadau vibhūṣaṇāny aṅge viśvakarmā cakāra ha ||104||**

**divya-mālyāmbara-dharā snātā bhūṣaṇa-bhūṣitā |**  
**paśyatāṁ sarva-devānāṁ yayau vakṣaḥ-sthalaṁ hareḥ ||105||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: paśyatāṁ sarvadevānāṁ tān anādṛtyety arthaḥ ||105||

**tayā vilokitā devā hari-vakṣaḥ-sthalasthayā |**  
**lakṣmyā maitreya sahasā parāṁ nirvṛtim āgatā ||106||**

**udvegaṁ paramaṁ jagmur daityā viṣṇu-parāṅ-mukhāḥ |**  
**tyaktā lakṣmyā mahā-bhāga vipratcitti-purogamāḥ ||107||**

**tatas te jagṛhur daityā dhanvantari-kara-sthitam |**  
**kamaṇḍaluṁ mahāvīryā yatrāste’mṛtam uttamam ||108||**

**māyayā mohá tān viṣṇuḥ strī-rūpa-saṁsthitaḥ |**  
**dānavebhyas tad ādāya devebhyaḥ pradadau prabhuḥ ||109||**

**tataḥ papuḥ sura-gaṇāḥ śarādyās tadāmṛtam |**  
**udyatāyudha-nistriṁśā daityās tāṁś ca samabhyayuḥ ||110||**

**pīte’mṛte ca balibhir devair daitya-camūs tadā |**  
**badhyamānā diśo bheje pāṭalaṁ ca viveśa vai ||111||**

**tato devā mudā yuktāḥ śaṅkha-cakra-gadā-bhṛtam |**  
**praṇipatya yathā-pūrvam āśāsat tat triviṣṭapam ||112||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tata iti || dravarūpamekaṁ dravyamamṛtaṁ jātam; anyat somātmakam ||100-112|| 

**tataḥ prasannabhāḥ sūryaḥ prayayau svena vartmanā |**  
**jyotīṁṣi ca yathā-mārgaṁ prayayur muni-sattama ||113||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: prasannabhāḥ spaṣṭadīptiḥ san svena vartmanā dakṣiṇottarāyaṇaniyamena | jyotīṁṣi tārāgrahabhaumādayo yathāmārgaṁ vakrāticāraṁ vinā ||113||

**jajvāla bhagavāṁś coccaiś cāru-dīptir vibhāvasuḥ |**  
**dharme ca sarva-bhūtānāṁ tadā matir ajāyata ||114||**

**trailokyaṁ ca śriyā juṣṭaṁ babhūva dvija-sattama |**  
**śakraś ca tridaśa-śreṣṭhaḥ punaḥ śrīmān ajāyata ||115||**

**siṁhāsana-gataḥ śakraḥ samprāpya tridivaṁ punaḥ |**  
**deva-rājye sthito devīṁ tuṣṭāvābja-karāṁ tataḥ ||116||\*\***

**śrīdharaḥ**: durvāsaḥśāpapātena punarmābhūdiyaṁ tathā | ityabhiprāyataḥ śakrastuṣṭāva śriyamānataḥ ||116|| 

**indra uvāca—[^4]**  
**namasye sarva-bhūtānāṁ[^5] jananīm abja-sambhavām |**  
**śriyam unnidra-padmākṣīṁ viṣṇu-vakṣaḥ-sthala-sthitām ||116||[^6]**

**śrīdharaḥ**: namasye namāmi sarva-bhūtānāṁ jananīṁ tvām ||116||

**tvaṁ siddhis tvaṁ svadhā svāhā sudhā tvaṁ loka-pāvanī |**  
**sandhyā rātriḥ prabhā bhūtir medhā śraddhā sarasvatī ||117||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tvaṁ siddhir aṇimādiḥ | prabhā divasaḥ ||117||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tata iti || svena vartmanā-ayanādivyatyāsaṁ vinā | yathāmārgaṁ-vakrāticāravarjam ||115-117|| 

**yajña-vidyā mahā-vidyā guhya-vidyā ca śobhate[^7] |**  
**ātma-vidyā ca devi tvaṁ vimukti-phala-dāyinī ||118||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yajña-vidyā karma-vidyā | mahā-vidyā viśva-rūpopāsanā | guhya-vidyā tad-vācaka-dvādaśākṣarādi-rahasya-mantra-vidyā | ātma-vidyā brahma-vidyā | evaṁ karma-vidyādi-rūpeṇa vimukti-phala-dāyinī tvam eva ||118||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** yajñeti || yajña-vidyā dharma-mīmāṁsā, mahāvidyā indrajālādi-kuhakajñānam | guhya-vidyā mantra-vāda-viśeṣaḥ ||118||

**ānvīkṣikī trayī vārtā daṇḍa-nītis tvam eva ca |**  
**saumyāsaumyair jagad-rūpais tvayaitad devi pūritam ||119||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kiṁ ca, ānvikṣikī tarka-vidyā tvam eva | trayī veda-trayaṁ vārtā śilpa-śāstrāyurvedādiḥ | daṇḍa-nītiḥ sāmādy-upāya-pratipādaka-rāja-nītiḥ | evam anyair api saumyāsaumyai rūpais tvadīyaiḥ etaj jagat pūritam ||119||

**kā tv anyā tvām ṛte devi sarva-yajña-mayaṁ vapuḥ |**  
**adhyāste deva-devasya yogi-cintyaṁ gadābhṛtaḥ ||120||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atas tava saubhāgyam atyāścaryam ity āha—kā tv iti | kā punas tvad-anyā yadābhṛto vapur adhyāste tad vakṣasi vasatīty arthaḥ ||120||

**tvayā devi parityaktaṁ sakalaṁ bhuvana-trayam |**  
**vinaṣṭa-prāyam abhavat tvayedānīṁ samedhitam ||121||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atas tad-upekṣānukampayor īdṛśaṁ phalaṁ dṛṣṭam ity āha—tvayeti | samedhitaṁ saṁvardhitam ||121||

**dārāḥ putrās tathāgāraṁ suhṛd-dhānya-dhanādikam |**  
**bhavaty etan mahā-bhāge nityaṁ tvad-vīkṣaṇān nṛṇām ||122||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tac caitat citram ity āha—dārā iti tribhiḥ ||122||

**śarīrārogyam aiśvaryam ari-pakṣa-kṣayaḥ sukham |**  
**devi tvad-dṛṣṭi-dṛṣṭānāṁ puruṣāṇāṁ ca durlabham ||123||**

**tvaṁ mātā sarva-lokānāṁ devadevo hariḥ pitā |**  
**tvayaitad viṣṇunā cāmba jagad vyāptaṁ carācaram ||124||**

**mā naḥ kośaṁ tathā goṣṭhaṁ mā gṛhaṁ mā paricchadam |**  
**mā śarīraṁ kalatraṁ ca tyajethāḥ sarva-pāpani ||125||**

**mā putrān mā suhṛd-vargaṁ mā paśūn mā vibhūṣaṇam |**  
**tyajethā mama devasya viṣṇor vakṣaḥ-sthalālaye ||126||**

**sattvena satya-śaucābhyāṁ tathā śīlādibhir guṇaiḥ |**  
**tyajyante te narāḥ sadyaḥ santyaktā ye tvayāmale ||127||**

**tvayāvalokitāḥ sadyaḥ śīlādyair akhilair guṇaiḥ |**  
**kulaiśvaryaiś ca yujyante puruṣā nirguṇā api ||128||**

**sa ślāghyaḥ saguṇī dhanya sakulīnaḥ sa buddhimān |**  
**sa śūraḥ sa ca vikrānto yas tvayā devi vīkṣitaḥ ||129||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ato mā tvaṁ no'smākaṁ kośādikaṁ tyajethāḥ | paricchadaṁ parikaram ||125-129|| 

**sadyo vaiguṇyam āyānti śīlādyāḥ sakalā guṇāḥ |**  
**parāṅmukhī jagaddhātrī yasya tvaṁ viṣṇu-vallabhe ||130||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tvayā ca parityaktānām aniṣṭaṁ bhavatītyāha, sadya iti | vaiguṇyaṁ doṣatvam ||130||

**na te varṇayituṁ śaktā guṇān jihvāpi vedhasaḥ |**  
**prasīda devi padmākṣi māsmāṁs tyākṣīḥ kadācana ||131||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atastadguṇastutau na ko'pi śaktaḥ, kṛpayaiva kevalaṁ prasīdeti prārthayate-na ta iti | vedhaso'pi jihvā na śaktetyanvayaḥ ||131|| 

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**evaṁ śrīḥ saṁstutā samyak prāha devī śatakratum |**  
**śṛṇvatāṁ sarva-devānāṁ sarva-bhūta-sthitā dvija ||132||**

**śrīr uvāca—**  
**parituṣṭāsmi deveśa stotreṇānena te hare |**  
**varaṁ vṛṇīṣva yas tv iṣṭo varadāhaṁ tavāgatā ||133||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: hare\! Indra ||133||

**indra uvāca—**  
**varadā yadi me devi varārho yadi vāpy aham |**  
**trailokyaṁ na tvayā tyājyam eṣa me’stu varaḥ paraḥ ||134||**

**stotreṇa yas tathaitena tvāṁ stoṣyaty abdhi-sambhave |**  
**sa tvayā na parityājyo dvitīyo’stu varo mama ||135||**

**śrīr uvāca—**  
**trailokyaṁ tridaśa-śreṣṭha na santyakṣyāmi vāsava |**  
**datto varo mayā yas te stotrārādhana-tuṣṭayā ||136||**

**yaś ca sāyaṁ tathā prātaḥ stotreṇānena mānavaḥ |**  
**māṁ stoṣyati sa tasyāhaṁ bhaviṣyāmi parāṅmukhī ||137||**

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**evaṁ varaṁ dadau devī devarājāya vai purā |**  
**maitreya śrīr mahā-bhāgā stotrārādhana-toṣitā ||138||**

**bhṛgoḥ khyātyāṁ samutpannā śrīḥ pūrvam udadheḥ punaḥ |**  
**deva-dānava-yatnena prasūtāmṛta-manthane ||139||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: prakṛtaṁ śriyo'vatāradvayaṁ nigamayan prasaṅgādanyānapi tadavatārānāha, bhṛgority-ādi yāvadadhyāyasamāptiḥ ||139|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** ānvīkṣikīti || ānvīkṣikī tarkaśāstram | daṇḍanītiḥ-arthaśāstram ||119-139||

**evaṁ yathā jagat-svāmī devadevo janārdanaḥ |**  
**avatāraṁ karoty eṣa tathā śrīs tat-sahāyinī ||140||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tatsahāyini tadanuvartanaśīlā ||140|| 

**punaś ca padmād udbhūtā ādityo’bhūd yadā hariḥ |**  
**yadā tu bhārgavo rāmas tadābhūd dharaṇī tv iyam ||141||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yadā harirādityo vāmano'bhūt | bhārgavo jāmadagnyaḥ ||141|| 

**rāghavatve’bhavat sītā rukmiṇī kṛṣṇa-janmani |**  
**anyeṣu cāvatāreṣu viṣṇor eṣā sahāyinī ||142||**

**devatve deva-deheyaṁ mānuṣatve ca mānuṣī |**  
**viṣṇor dehānurūpāṁ vai karoty eṣātmanas tanum ||143||**

**yaś caiutac chṛṇyāj janma lakṣmyā yaś ca paṭhen naraḥ |**  
**śriyo na vicyutis tasya gṛhe yāvat kula-trayam ||144||**

**pāthyate yeṣu caivaiṣa gṛheṣu śrī-stavo mune |**  
**alakṣmīḥ kalahādhārā na teṣv āste kadācana ||145||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kalahādhārā kalaha ādhāro yasyāḥ sā kalaho'pi teṣu na bhavatīty arthaḥ ||145|| 

iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśābhidhāyāṁ viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ prathamāṁśe navamo'dhyāyaḥ |

**etat te kathitaṁ brahman yan māṁ tvaṁ paripṛcchasi |**  
**kṣīrābdhau śrīr yathā jātā pūrvaṁ bhṛgu-sutā satī ||146||**

**iti sakala-vibhūty-avāpti-hetuḥ**  
**stutir iyam indra-mukhodgatā hi lakṣmyāḥ |**  
**anudinam iha paṭhyate nṛbhir yair**  
**vasati na teṣu kadācid apy alakṣmīḥ ||147||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** evam iti || tatsahāyinī-tena saha ayate gacchatīti tatsahāyinī, tatsahacāriṇīty arthaḥ ||140-147|| 

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe prathame’ṁśe navamo’dhyāyaḥ   
||9||

—o)0(o—

(1.10)



## **bhṛgu-sargādīnāṁ punaḥ kathanam**

**śrī-maitreya uvāca—**  
**kathitaṁ me tvayā sarvaṁ yat pṛṣṭho’si mayā mune |**  
**bhṛgu-sargāt prabhṛty eṣa sargo me kathyatāṁ punaḥ ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: punarbhṛgusargāt prabhṛti bhṛgusutānuvādapūrvakameṣa bhṛrgovaṁśa, kathyatām, anyathā pūrvāparakathāsambandhāpratīterity arthaḥ ||1||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** atha saṁkṣepeṇa śrutaṁ bhṛgusargaṁ vistarataḥ śrotuṁ pṛcchati kathitam iti ||1|| 

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**bhṛgoḥ khyātyāṁ samutpannā lakṣmīr viṣṇu-parigrahaḥ |**  
**tathā dhātṛ-vidhātārau khyātyāṁ jātau sutau bhṛgoḥ ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: ato bhṛgoḥ sutān anuvadati bhṛgor iti | viṣṇoḥ parigrahaḥ patnī ||2|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** bhṛgor iti || parigrahaḥ-kalatram ||2|| 

**āyatir niyatiś caiva meroḥ kanye mahātmanaḥ |**  
**bhārye dhātṛ-vidhātros te tayor jātau sutāv ubhau ||3||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** āyatiriti || tayoḥ-āyatiniyatyoḥ, sutāvubhau jātau ||3||

**prāṇaś caiva mṛkaṇḍuś ca mārkaṇḍeyo mṛkaṇḍutaḥ |**  
**tato veda-śirā jajñe prāṇasyāpi sutaṁ śṛṇu ||4||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tābhyāṁ tayor āyati-niyatyoḥ pratyekaṁ prāṇāś ca mṛkaṇḍaścety evam ubhau sutau jātāvity anvayaḥ | prāṇasya vedaśirā yajñe ity anvayaḥ ||3-4||

**prāṇasya dyutmān putro rājavāṁś ca tato’bhavat |**  
**tato vaṁśo mahābhāga vistaraṁ bhārgavo gataḥ ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasyaiva putrāntaramāha prāṇasyeti ||5||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** tāvevāha prāṇaś ceti || prāṇo mṛkaṇḍuś ca | tatra mṛkaṇḍuto mārkaṇḍeyo jajña ity anvayaḥ | (tayor jātāviti pāṭhaḥ) ||4-5||

**patnī marīceḥ sambhūtiḥ paurṇamāsam asūyata |**  
**virajāḥ parvataś caiva tasya putrau mahātmanaḥ ||6||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tad evaṁ caturviṁśatidakṣakanyānāṁ madhye śradvādīnāṁ trayodaśānāṁ dharmabhāryāṇāṁ vaṁśāḥ kathitāḥ | anantarañca khyātiḥ satyatha sambhūtirityuddiṣṭānām ekādaśānāṁ bhṛgumarīcyādibhāryāṇāṁ madhye khyātyāṁ bhṛgorvaṁśo nirūpitaḥ | satyāś ca bhavabhāryāyā dakṣakopād aprauḍhāyā evaṁ dehatyāgoktyā tasyā vaṁśo nābhūdity arthaduktam | atha kramaprāptaṁ marīceḥ sambhūtyāṁ jātaṁ vaṁśamāha patnī marīceriti ||6||

**vaṁśa-saṁkīrtane putrān vadiṣye’haṁ tato dvija |**  
**smṛtiś cāṅgirasaḥ patnī prasūtā kanyakās tathā |**  
**sinīvālī kuhūś caiva rākā cānumatis tathā ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vaṁśasaṅkīrtana iti | marīcer eva kaśyapo'nyaḥ putraḥ, tat putrā vivasvadādayaḥ | ityasminnevāṁśe ante vaṁśakīrtane vakṣye vivasvataḥ śrāddhadevādayaḥ | śrāddhadevasya ikṣvākupramukhā ity-ādi tattat putrān vistarato vaṁśīkīrtane caturthāṁśe vakṣye | atra tu svalpatvāt paurṇamāsānvayamātramuktam itvarthaḥ ||7|| 

**anasūyā tathaivātrer jajñe niṣkalmaṣān sutān |**  
**somaṁ durvāsasaṁ caiva dattātreyaṁ ca yoginam ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tāḥ kanyā nirdiśati sinīvālīti ||8||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** atha kamaprāptaṁ marīceḥ saṁbhūtyāṁ jātaṁ vaṁśam āha—panī marīceriti || atrālpasantāno marīceḥ putraḥ paurṇamāsa uktaḥ | bahusantānān kāśyapavivasvadādīnputrapautrādīnasminnaṁśe vaṁśasaṁkīrtane ādityotpattiprastāve turīryeśe sūryavaṁśaprastāve ca vakṣye ||6-8|| 

**prītyāṁ pulastya-bhāryāyāṁ dattolis tat-suto’bhavat |**  
**pūrva-janmani yo’gastyaḥ smṛtaḥ svāyambhuve’ntare ||9||**

**kardamaś corvarīyāṁś ca sahiṣṇuś ca sutās trayaḥ |**  
**kṣamā tu suṣuve bhāryā pulahasya prajāpateḥ ||10||**

**kretāś ca santatir bhāryā vālakhilyān asūyata |**  
**ṣaṣṭi-putra-sahasrāṇi munīnām ūrdhva-retasām |**  
**aṅguṣṭha-parva-mātrāṇāṁ jvalad-bhāskara-tejasām ||11||**

**ūrjāyāṁ tu vasiṣṭhasya saptājāyanta vai sutāḥ ||12||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** prītyām iti || tatsutaḥ-tasya pulastyasya aurasaḥ sutaḥ ||9-12|| 

**rajo gotrordhvabāhuś ca savanaś cānaghas tathā |**  
**sutapāḥ śukra ity ete sarve saptarṣayo’malāḥ ||13||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** raja iti || saptarṣaya iti | ete tṛtīye manvantare saptarṣayo vakṣyante ||13||

**yo’sāv agny-abhimānī syāt brahmaṇas tanayo’grajaḥ |**  
**tasmāt svāhā sutān lebhe trīn udāraujaso dvija ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: saptarṣayastṛtīye manvantare | abhimānī devaḥ na tu jvalanamātrarūpaḥ brahmaṇastanayo'grajaḥ mukhānagnirajāyata iti śruteḥ ||14||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** sargaprasaṁgādagnisargamāha yo'sāviti ||14||

**pāvakaṁ pavamānaṁ tu śuciṁ cāpi jalāśinam ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: udāraujasaḥ atitejasvinaḥ jalāśinaṁ sūryasthatvāt | tathā ca kaurme 

nirmathyaḥ pavamānaḥ syād vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ |   
yaścāsau tapate sūrye śuciragnirasau smṛtaḥ iti ||15||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** pāvakam iti || yathā kaume 

nirmanthyaḥ pavamānaḥ syādvaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ ||   
yaścāsau tapate sūrye śuciragnirasau smṛtaḥ || iti | 

jalāśinam iti śuciviśeṣaṇam ||15||

**teṣāṁ tu santatāv anye catvāriṁśac ca pañca ca |**  
**kathyante vahnayaś caite pitā-putra-trayaṁ ca yat ||16||**

**evam ekonapañcāśad vahnayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||17||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** teṣām iti || pitṛputratrayaṁ-pitā putratrayaṁ ca, trayaḥ putrāḥ pratyekaṁ pañcadaśaputrakāḥ ||16-17|| 

**pitaro brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā vyākhyātā ye mayā dvija |**  
**agniṣv āttā barhiṣado’nagnayaḥ sāgnayaś ca ye ||18||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: teṣāṁ trayāṇāṁ pratyekaṁ pañcadaśa, pañcacatvāriṁśad vahnayaḥ | pitā brahmaputra ekastat putratrayaṁ pāvakādi | evamekonapañcāśat ||18||

**tebhyaḥ svadhā sute jajñe menāṁ vai dhāriṇīṁ tathā |**  
**te ubhe brahma-vādinyau yoginyāv apy ubhe dvija ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: agniṣvāttā anadyayo jātāḥ | barhiṣadaḥ sāgnayo yajvānaḥ | ye vā ayajvāno gṛhabhedhinaḥ te pitaro'gniṣvātāḥ | ye vai yajvānaste pitaro barhiṣadaḥ iti śruteḥ ||19|| 

**uttama-jñāna-sampanne sarvaiḥ samuditair guṇaiḥ ||20||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** pitara iti || agniṣvāttāḥ-ayajvāno, mūrrāstrayo gaṇāḥ | barhiṣadaḥ-yajvāno mūrtimantaścatvāraḥ | agniśvāttasutā menā ||18-20||

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇavyākhyāne śrī-viṣṇucittīye prathame'ṁśe daśamo'dhyāyaḥ ||10||

**ity eṣā dakṣa-kanyānāṁ kathitāpatya-santatiḥ |**  
**śraddhāvān saṁsmarann etām anapatnyo na jāyate ||21||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tayor vivāhādikaṁ na abhūd ityāśayena āha, te ubhe iti ||19-20|| 

iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśābhidhāyāṁ viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ prathamāṁśe daśamo'dhyāyaḥ |

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe prathame’ṁśe daśamo’dhyāyaḥ   
||10||

—o)0(o—

(1.11)



## **dhruvopākhyānam**

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**priyavratottānapādau manoḥ svāyambhuvasya tu |**  
**dvau putrau tu mahāvīryau dharmajñau kathitau tava ||1||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: manoḥ kanyānvayaḥ proktaḥ putravaṁśo'dhunocyate | tatrādhyāyadvayenāha dhruvasya caritaṁ mahat | manordvau putrau dve ca kanye | tatra kanyayor vaṁśa uktaḥ | idānīṁ putradvayānuvādapūrvakamuttānapādavaṁśamāha, prīyavratetyādinā ||1||

**tayor uttānapādasya surucyām uttamaḥ sutaḥ |**  
**abhīṣṭāyām abhūd brahman pitur atyanta-vallabhaḥ ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasya suruciḥ sunītiś ceti dve bhārye | tatra surucyām abhīṣṭāyāṁ preyasyām uttamo nāma suto'bhūt ||2||

**sunītir nāma yā rājñas tasyāsīn mahiṣī dvija |**  
**sa nātiprītimāṁs tasyām abhūd yasyā dhruvaḥ sutaḥ ||3||**

**rājāsana-sthitasyāṅkaṁ pitur bhrātaram āśritam |**  
**dṛṣṭottamaṁ dhruvaś cakre tam āroḍhuṁ manoratham ||4||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: rājāsanasthitasya pituraṅkam utsaṅgamāśritaṁ bhrātaram uttamaṁ dṛṣṭvā, tamaṅkam āroḍhuṁ dhruvo manorathaṁ cakre ity anvayaḥ ||4||

**pratyakṣaṁ bhūpatis tasyāḥ surucyā nābhyanandata |**  
**praṇayenāgataṁ putram utsaṅgārohaṇotsukam ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: surucyāḥ preyasyāḥ pratyakṣaṁ samakṣaṁ tatpraṇayabhaṅgabhayād dhruvaṁ na abhyanandat ||5||

**sapatnī-tanayaṁ dṛṣṭvā tam aṅkārohaṇotsukam |**  
**sva-putraṁ ca tathārūḍhaṁ surucir vākyam abravīt ||6||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: taṁ dhruvaṁ pituraṅkārohaṇotsukaṁ dṛṣṭvā tathā svaputrañca tadaṅkārūḍhaṁ dṛṣṭvā surucirabravīt ity anvayaḥ ||6||

**kriyate kiṁ vṛthā vatsa mahān eṣa manorathaḥ |**  
**anya-strī-garbha-jātena hy asambhūta mamodare ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: surucyā duruktim asahamāno dhruvaḥstrījitaṁ pitaraṁ vihāya mātuḥ samīpaṁ gatvā duḥkhitāyāstasyā anumatyā purānnirgatya saptarṣīṇām upadeśena madhuvane bhagavantam ārādhya padaṁ prāpta iti krameṇa kathayiṣyan surucyā garvoktimāha, kriyate kim iti caturbhiḥ ||7||

**uttamottamam aprāpyam aviveko hi vāñchasi |**  
**satyaṁ sutas tvam apy asya kintu na tvaṁ mayā dhṛthaḥ ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: aviveko mandamatiḥ ||8|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** manaurdauhitro vaṁśaḥ uktaḥ | atha tatputrānvayaṁ vaktumanuvadati priyavrateti ||1-8|| 

**etad rājāsanaṁ sarva-bhū-bhṛt-saṁśraya-ketanam |**  
**yogyaṁ mamaiva putrasya kim ātmā kliśyate tvayā ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: etad rājāsanaṁ sarvabhūbhṛtāṁ saṁśrayasya cakravartinaḥ ketanaṁ sthānaṁ matputrasyaiva yogyaṁ na hi rājaputratāmātralabhyam etat kintu madgarbhasambhavasaubhāgyalabhyam ||9|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** etaditi || pūrvoktam uttamatvamāha sarvetiv|| sarvabhūbhṛdāśrayaketanam iti ca pāṭhaḥv| sarvabhūbhṛtāmāśrayasya sarvabhaumasya ketanaṁ sthānam ||9|| 

**uccair manorathas te’yaṁ mat-putrasyeva kiṁ vṛthā |**  
**sunītyām ātmano janma kiṁ tvayā nāvagamyate ||10||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: atastava ayamuccaiḥ utkṛṣṭaiśvaryyamanoratho vṛthaiva, ityatigarvoktiḥ ||10||

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**utsṛjya pitaraṁ bālas tac chrutvā mātṛ-bhāṣitam |**  
**jagāma kupito mātur nijāyā dvija mandiram ||11||**

**taṁ dṛṣṭvā kupitaṁ putram īṣat prasphuritādharam |**  
**sunītir aṅkam āropya maitreyedam abhāṣata ||12||**

**vatsa kaḥ kopa-hetus te kaś ca tvāṁ nābhinandati |**  
**ko’vajānāti pitaraṁ vatsa yas te’parādhyati ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yaste aparādhyati aparādhaṁ karoti, sa tava pitaram eva avajānāti | sa caivambhūtaḥ kaḥ ity arthaḥ ||13||

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**ity uktaḥ sakalaṁ mātre kathayāmāsa tad yathā |**  
**suruciḥ prāha bhūpāla-pratyakṣam atigarvitā ||14||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** ucairiti || uccairmanorathaḥ-uccāsanāmilāpaḥ ||10-14||

**viniḥśvasyeti kathite tasmin putreṇa durmanāḥ |**  
**śvāsa-kṣāmekṣaṇā dīnā sunītir vākyam abravīt ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasmin surucyā vacasi kathite sati śvāsena atyuṣṇena kṣāme mlāne īkṣaṇe netre yasyāḥ ||15|| 

**sunītir uvāca—**  
**suruciḥ satyam āhedaṁ mandabhāgyo’si putraka |**  
**na hi puṇyavatāṁ vatsa sapatnair evam ucyate ||16||**

**nodvegas tāta kartavyaḥ kṛtaṁ yad bhavatā purā |**  
**tat ko’pahartuṁ śaknoti dātuṁ kaś cākṛtaṁ tvayā ||17||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: udvegaḥ kṣobhaḥ ||17|| 

**tat tvayā nātra kartavyaṁ duḥkhaṁ tad-vākya-sambhavam ||18||**

**rājāsanaṁ rāja-cchatraṁ varāśva-vara-vāraṇāḥ |**  
**yasya puṇyāni tasyaite matvaitac chāmya putraka ||19||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: etanmatvā avabudhya śāmya upaśamaṁ bhaja ||19|| 

**anya-janma-kṛtaiḥ puṇyaiḥ surucyāṁ surucir nṛpaḥ |**  
**bhāryeti procyate cānyā mad-vidhā puṇya-varjitā ||20||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: surucyāṁ nṛpaḥ suruciḥ atiprītimān | madvidhā mādṛśī tu kevalaṁ bhāryeti procyate ||20|| 

**puṇyopacaya-sampannas tasyāḥ putras tathottamaḥ |**  
**mama putras tathā jātaḥ svalpa-puṇyo dhruvo bhavān ||21||**

**tathāpi duḥkhaṁ na bhavān kartum arhati putraka |**  
**yasya yāvat sa tenaiva svena tuṣyati mānavaḥ ||22||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yasya yāvadeva prāptaṁ sa tena tuṣyati ||22|| 

**yadi te duḥkham aty arthaṁ surucyā vacasābhavat |**  
**tat-puṇyopacaye yatnaṁ kuru sarva-phala-prade ||23||**

**suśīlo bhava dharmātmā maitraḥ prāṇihite rataḥ |**  
**nimnaṁ yathāpaḥ pravaṇāḥ pātram āyānti sampadaḥ ||24||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: maitro mitradharmā | pravaṇāḥ nimnadeśābhimukhyaḥ satyaḥ pātraṁ saguṇaṁ naram ||24||

**dhruva uvāca—**  
**amba yat tvam idaṁ prāttha praśamāya vaco mama |**  
**naitad durvacasā bhinne hṛdaye mama tiṣṭhati ||25||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: amba\! he mātaḥ\! mama praśamāya nodvegastāta karttavya ity-ādi saptaślokīrūpaṁ yad vacaḥ prāha bravīṣi, tad bhinne bhāṇḍe paya iva mama hṛdaye na tiṣṭhati ||25||

**so’haṁ tathā yatiṣyāmi yathā sarvottamottamam |**  
**sthānaṁ prāpsyāmy aśeṣāṇāṁ jagatām abhipūjitam ||26||**

**surucir dayitā rājñas tasyā jāto’smi nodarāt |**  
**prabhāvaṁ paśya me’mba tvaṁ vṛddhasyāpi tavodare ||27||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vṛddhasya vṛddhiṁ prāptasyāpi ||27||

**uttamaḥ sa mama bhrātā yo garbheṇa dhṛtas tayā |**  
**sa rājāsanam āpnotu pitrā dattaṁ tathāstu tat ||28||**

**nānya-dattam abhīpsāmi sthānam amba sva-karmaṇā |**  
**icchāmi tad ahaṁ sthānaṁ yan na prāpa pitā mama ||29||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kintu svakarmaṇā prāptum eva icchāmi || 29|| 

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**nirjagāma gṛhān mātur ity uktvā mātaraṁ dhruvaḥ |**  
**purāc ca nirgamya tatas tad bāhyopavanaṁ yayau ||30||**

**sa dadarśa munīṁs tatra sapta pūrvāgatān dhruvaḥ |**  
**kṛṣṇājinottarīyeṣu viṣṭareṣu samāsthitān ||31||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: pūrvāgatān svānugrahāya tataḥ pūrvam eva tatrāgatān kṛṣṇājinam uttarīyamupari āstaraṇaṁ yeṣāṁ teṣu viṣṭareṣu kuśāsaneṣu upaviṣṭān ||31||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** niḥśvasyeti | tasmin vṛttānte kathite sati, śvāsakṣāmekṣaṇā-śvāsena duḥkhajānetena kṛśadṛṣṭiḥ ||15-31|| 

**sa rāja-putras tān sarvān prāṇipatyābhyabhāṣata |**  
**praśrayāvanataḥ samyag abhivācana-pūrvakam ||32||**

**dhruva uvāca—**  
**uttānapāda-tanayaṁ māṁ nibodhata sattamāḥ |**  
**jātaṁ sunītyāṁ nirvedād yuṣmākaṁ prāptam antikam ||33||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: nirvedāt duḥkhāt prāptaṁ jānīta ity arthaḥ ||33||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** sa iti || pūrvāgatāṁ-pūrvamevātmano'nugrahaṇārthamāgatān, kṛṣṇājinottarīyāṇyeva viṣṭharāsteṣu ||32-33|| 

**ṛṣaya ūcuḥ—**  
**catuḥ-pañcābda-sambhūto bālas tvaṁ nṛpa-nandana |**  
**nirveda-kāraṇaṁ kiñcit tava nādyāpi vartate ||34||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: catvāraḥ pañca vā abdā yasya, sa cāsau sambhūtaś ca samyagbhūtaḥ saukumāryeṇa jātaḥ | alpavayāḥ komalataraścety  arthaḥ ||34||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** catuḥpaṁceti || itaḥ prāk caturthe paṁcame vā'nde saṁbhūtaḥ ||34||

**na cintyaṁ bhavataḥ kiñcid dhriyate bhūpatiḥ pitā**   
**na caiveṣṭa-viyogādi tava paśyāma bālaka ||35||**

**śarīre na ca te vyādhir asmābhir upalakṣyate |**  
**nirvedaḥ kiṁ-nimittas te kathyatāṁ yadi vidyate ||36||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: cintyaṁ kuṭumbādiviṣayaṁ bhavataḥ kiñcinnāsti, yataḥ pitā dhriyate jīvati | sa ca bhūpatiḥ ||36||

**śrī-parāśara uvāca—**  
**tataḥ sa kathayāmāsa surucyā yad udāhṛtam |**  
**tan niśamya tataḥ procur munayas te parasparam ||37||**

**aho kṣātraṁ paraṁ tejo bālasyāpi yad akṣamā |**  
**sapatnyā mātur uktaṁ yad dhṛdayān nāpasarpati ||38||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: akṣamā mānabhaṅgāsahanam ||38|| 

**bho bho kṣatriya-dāyāda nirvedād yat tvayādhunā |**  
**kartuṁ vyavasitaṁ tan naḥ kathyatāṁ yadi rocate ||39||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kṣatriyadāyāda\! kṣatriyaputra ||39|| 

**yac ca kāryaṁ tavāsmābhiḥ sāhāyyam amita-dyute |**  
**tad ucyatāṁ vivakṣus tvam asmābhir upalakṣyase ||40||**

**dhruva uvāca—**  
**nāham artham abhīpsāmi na rājyaṁ dvija-sattamāḥ |**  
**tat sthānam ekam icchāmi bhuktaṁ nānyena yat purā ||41||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vivakṣuḥ kiñcid vaktumicchuḥ ||40-41||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** neti || cintyaṁ-kuṭumbapoṣaṇādi | dhriyate-jīvati ||35-41|| 

**etan me kriyatāṁ samyak kathyatāṁ prāpyate yathā |**  
**sthānam agryaṁ samastebhyaḥ sthānebhyo muni-sattamāḥ ||42||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: etat sāhāyyaṁ kriyatām | sāhāyyaprākaramevāha samyak kathyatām iti ||42||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** etaditi || yathā prāpyate tathā kathyatām | etatkathanam eva sāhāyyaṁ tatkriyatām ||42||

**marīcir uvāca—**  
**anārādhita-govindair naraiḥ sthānaṁ nṛpātmaja |**  
**na hi samprāpyate śreṣṭhaṁ tasmād ārādhayācyutam ||43||**

**atrir uvāca—**  
**paraḥ parāṇāṁ puruṣo yasya tuṣṭo janārdanaḥ |**  
**sa prāpnoty akṣayaṁ sthānam etat satyaṁ mayoditam ||44||**

**aṅgirā uvāca—**  
**yasyāntaḥ sarvam evedam acyutasyāvyayātmanaḥ |**  
**tam ārādhaya govindaṁ sthānam agryaṁ yadīcchasi ||45||**

**pulastya uvāca—**  
**paraṁ brahma paraṁ dhāma yo’sau brahma tathā param |**  
**tam ārādhya hariṁ yāti muktim apy atidurlabhām ||46||**

**pulaha uvāca—**  
**aindram indraḥ paraṁ sthānaṁ yam ārādhya jagat-patim |**  
**prāpa yajñapatiṁ viṣṇuṁ tam ārādhaya suvrata ||47||**

**kratur uvāca—**  
**yo yajña-puruṣo yajñe yoge ca paramaḥ pumān |**  
**tasmiṁs tuṣṭe yad aprāpyaṁ kiṁ tad asti janārdane ||48||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** bhagavati bhaktyatiśayāt dhruve kāruṇyācca sarve'pi prativadanti praṇandanti ca anārādhitetyādi saptabhiḥ ||43-48|| 

**vasiṣṭha uvāca—**  
**prāpnoṣy ārādhite viṣṇau manasā yad yad icchasi |**  
**trailokyāntar-gataṁ sthānaṁ kim u vastottamottamam ||49||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: manasā yad yadicchati, satyalokādi tadapi prāpnoti | trailokyāntargatamuttamaṁ prāpnotīti kimu vaktavyam ||49||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** prāmoṣīti || manaseti | itaḥ pūrvamakḷptam api dadāti kiṁ punaḥ kḷptam iti ||49||

**dhruva uvāca—**  
**ārādhyaḥ kathito devo bhavadbhir praṇatasya me |**  
**mayā tat-paritoṣāya yaj japtavyaṁ tad ucyatām ||50||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** ārādhya iti | bhayeti | anupanītasyāpyātmano yogyaṁ japyaṁ pṛcchati japtavyam iti ||50||

**yathā cārādhanaṁ tasya mayā kāryaṁ mahātmanaḥ |**  
**prasāda-sumukhās tan me kathayantu maharṣayaḥ ||51||**

**ṛṣaya ūcuḥ—**  
**rāja-putra yathā viṣṇottamr ārādhana-parair naraiḥ |**  
**kāryam ārādhanaṁ tan no yathāvac chrotum arhasi ||52||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kṛṣṇārādhanamevaikaṁ puṁsāṁ sarvaphalapradam | sarvairapyevamevokte tadupāyaṁ bubhutsate | ārādhyaḥ kathita iti dvābhyām ||50-52||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** yatheti japāṅgapraśnaḥ ||51-52||

**bāhyathārthaād akhilāc cittaṁ tyājayet prathamaṁ naraḥ |**  
**tasminn eva jagad-dhāmni tataḥ kurvīta niścalam ||53||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: brāhyārthānity-ādinā aṣṭāṅgayogasādhyacittasamādhānapūrvakaṁ mantrajapam upadiśanti | tatra prathamaṁ brāhyārthān citaṁ tyājayet iti tyāgānukūlaprāthamikaprayatnavidhānena yathārhaṁ yamaniyamāsanaprāṇāyāmapūrvakaḥ pratyāhāra uktaḥ | tasminneva niścalaṁ kurvīteti dhāraṇoktā ||53||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** cittaikāgratārūpo yogo japasyāṅgam iti sayogaṁ japyamupadiśanti bāhyeti tribhiḥ | bāhyārthād iti | bāhyārthāccittaṁ tyājayediti hiṁsānṛtādiniṣiddhatyāgarūpo yamaḥ, sarvaviṣayatyāgarūpaḥ pratyāhāraśroktaḥ; niścalaṁ kurvītetyāsanaprāṇāyāmau, tadadhīnatvāñcittasthairyasya; tasminneveti śubhāśraye dhāraṇā ||53||

**evam ekāgra-cittena tanmayena dhṛtātmanā |**  
**japtavyaṁ yan nibodhaitat tan naḥ pārthiva-nandana ||54||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: evamanena prakāreṇa ekāgracittena iti pūrvoktaṣaḍaṅgasādhyaṁ dhyānamuktam | tathā ca vakṣyati 

tadrūpa pratyayaivaikā santatiścānyanispṛhā |   
taddhyānaṁ prathamairaṅgaiḥ ṣaḍbhirniṣpādyate nṛpa | 

iti tanmayeneti samādhirukteḥ | dhṛtātmaneti punarlayavikṣepaprāptau tatparihārāya cittasthairye prayalaḥ uktaḥ taduktaṁ gītāsu 

yato yato niḥsarati manaścañcalamasthiram |   
tatastato niyamyaitadātmanyeva vaśaṁ nayet | iti ||54||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** evam iti || dhṛtātmaneti | yathārhaṁ śaucādiṣu kṛtayaneneti niyamaḥ, ekāgracitteneti dhyānam, tanmayeneti samādhiḥ, ityaṣṭāṅgayoga uktaḥ | tasya maitreya yogina iti hi yogitvaṁ vakṣyati ||54||

**hiraṇyagarbha-puruṣa-pradhānāvyakta-rūpiṇe |**  
**oṁ namo vāsudevāya śuddha-jñāna-svarūpiṇe ||55||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: hiraṇyagarbho brahmā, puruṣo viṣṇuḥ pradhīyate prakṣīpyate prakṛtau viśvamaneneti pralayahetuḥ śivaḥ pradhānasaṁjñaḥ avyaktasteṣāṁ trayāṇāṁ niyantā triguṇamāyāśaktikāraṇātmā | pāṭhāntare vyaktaṁ  
viśvam | etāni rūpāni santi yasya tasmai | evamaupādhikeṣu rūpeṣu satsvapi śuddhajñānātmakaḥ svabhāvo'pracyuta evāsti yasya tasmai | oṁkārapratipādyāya vāsudevāya nama iti mantrārthaḥ ||54|| 

iti śrīdhara-svāmi-kṛtāyām ātma-prakāśābhidhāyāṁ viṣṇu-purāṇa-ṭīkāyāṁ prathamāṁśe ekādaśo'dhyāyaḥ

**etaj jajāpa bhagavān japyaṁ svāyambhuvo manuḥ |**  
**pitāmahas tava purā tasya tuṣṭo janārdanaḥ ||56||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** hiraṇyeti || 

hiraṇyamasya garbho'bhūddhiraṇyasyāpi garbhajaḥ |   
tasmāddhiravyagarbha taṁ purāṇajñāḥ pracakṣire || 

iti bhārate hiraṇyagarbhaśabdaniruktyā hiraṇmayaṁ brahmāṇḍaṁ garbhe yasya saḥ hiraṇyagarbhaḥ; sa cātra puruṣādisamabhivyāhārātkālātmā jñeyaḥ | hiraṇyagarbhaḥ vyaṣṭiḥ, puruṣassamaṣṭiriti kecit | atra dvādaśākṣaramantro vivakṣitaḥ, laiṅgādiṣu dhruvasya tanmantropadeśaprasiddheḥ | sa tu rahasyupadeṣṭavyatvādatra yathāpāṭhe na paṭhitaḥ ||55-56||

**dadau yathābhilaṣitāṁ siddhiṁ trailokya-durlabhām |**  
**tathā tvam api govindaṁ toṣayaitat sadā japan ||57||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** dadāviti || tathā tvam iti | kuladevatāmaṁtro hi śīghraṁ siddhyati ||57|| 

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇavyākhyāne viṣṇucittīye prathame'ṁśe ekādaśo'dhyāyaḥ ||11||

iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe prathame’ṁśe ekādaśo’dhyāyaḥ   
||11||

 —o)0(o—

(1.12)



## **dhruvasya vara-lābhaḥ**

**parāśara uvāca—**  
**niśamya tad-aśeṣeṇa maitreya nṛpateḥ sutaḥ |**  
**nirjagāma vanāt tasmāt praṇipatya sa tān ṛṣīn ||1||**  
**kṛtakṛtyam ivātmānaṁ manyamānas tato dvija |**  
**madhu-saṁjñaṁ mahā-puṇyaṁ jagāma yamunā-taṭam ||2||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tasmāt puropavanād nirjagāma ||2||

**punaś ca madhu-saṁjñena daityenādhiṣṭhitaṁ yataḥ |**  
**tato madhuvanaṁ nāmnā khyātam atra mahītale ||3||**  
**hatvā ca lavaṇaṁ rakṣo-madhu-putraṁ mahā-balam |**  
**śatrughno mathurāṁ nāma purīṁ tatra cakāra vai ||4||**  
**yatra vai deva-devasya sānnidhyaṁ hari-medhasaḥ |**  
**sarva-pāpa-hare tasmiṁs tapas tīrthe cakāra saḥ ||5||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: haratīti hariḥ | sarva-duḥkha-hāriṇī yad-viṣayā medhā sa hari-medhāḥ | nityam asi ca prajā-medhayor iti sāntatvam ||5||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** yatreti || **hari-medhasaḥ** hariḥ pāpa-hāriṇī svarṇavat śuddhā medhā yasya, sa harimedhāḥ, tasya harimedhasaḥ | chāndasatvād asic-pratyayaḥ ||1-5||

**marīci-mukhyair[^8] munibhir yathoddiṣṭam abhūt tathā |**  
**ātmany aśeṣa-deveśaṁ sthitaṁ viṣṇum amanyata ||6||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: **marīci-mukhyair** marīci-pramukhaiḥ | **yathā uddiṣṭam** upadiṣṭam | **amanyata** dadhyau ||6|| 

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** marīci-miśrair iti || amanyata-dadhyau ||6|| 

**ananya-cetasas tasya dhyāyato bhagavān hariḥ |**  
**sarva-bhūta-gato vipra sarva-bhāva-gato’bhavat ||7||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: **sarva-bhāva-gataḥ** sarva-bhāvena viśva-rūpeṇa tac-cittatvaṁ gataḥ prāpto’bhavat ||7||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** ananya-cetasa iti || sarva-bhāva-gataḥ citta-vṛtteḥ sākalyena viṣayatayā'virbhūtaḥ ||7|| 

**manasy avasthite tasya viṣṇau maitreya yoginaḥ |**  
**na śaśāka dharā bhāram udvoḍhuṁ bhūta-dhāriṇī ||8||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tataś ca tasya bhāram udvoḍhuṁ bhūr-nāśaknod ity āha—manasy avasthita iti tribhiḥ ||8||

**vāma-pāda-sthite tasmin nanāmārdhena medinī |**  
**dvitīyaṁ ca nanāmārdhaṁ kṣiter dakṣiṇa-saṁsthite ||9||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: vāmena pādena sthite tasmin ardhena ardhaṁ vāma-bhāgato medinī nanāma avanatābhūt | dakṣiṇena pādena sthite tasmin kṣiter dvitīyaṁ dakṣiṇam ardhaṁ nanāma ||9||

**pādāṅguṣṭhena sampīḍya yadā sa vasudhāṁ sthitaḥ |**  
**tadā sā vasudhā vipra cacāla saha parvataiḥ ||10||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: yadā ca pādāṅguṣṭhena vasudhāṁ madhyataḥ sampīḍya ākramya sthitaḥ, tadā samastā vasudhā cacāla ||10||

**nadyo nadāḥ samudrāś ca saṁkṣobhaṁ paramaṁ yayuḥ |**  
**tat kṣobhād amarāḥ kṣobhaṁ paraṁ jagmur mahā-mune ||11||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: nadyādayaś ca kṣobhaṁ prāptāḥ ||11||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** manasīti || na śaśāketi | garimākhyasiddhirāsīdityarthaḥ ||8-11|| 

**yāmā nāma tadā devā maitreya paramākulāḥ |**  
**indreṇa saha saṁmantrya dhyāna-bhaṅgaṁ pracakramuḥ ||12||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: tato devair anekadhā vighne kriyamāṇe’pi tat-saṁhiter avyutthāna-lakṣaṇaṁ mati-dārḍhyam āha—yāmā nāmety-ādinā | evaṁ sarvāsu māyāsv ity ataḥ prāktanena granthena ||12||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** yāmā iti || yāmāḥ-svāyaṁbhuvamanvantare devāḥ ||12|| 

**kuṣmāṇḍā vividhai rūpaiḥ sahasreṇa mahā-mune |**  
**saṁhiti-bhaṅgam atyantam ārabdhāḥ kartum āturāḥ ||13||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: kuṣmāṇḍāḥ kecid upadevāḥ ||13||

**sunītir nāma tan-mātā sāsrā tat-purataḥ sthitā |**  
**putreti karuṇāṁ vācam āha māyā-mayī tadā ||14||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sāsnā āśrumukhī satī ||14||

**putrakāsmān nivartasva śarīra-vyaya-dāruṇāt |**  
**nirbandhanto mayā labdho bahubhis tvaṁ manorathaiḥ ||15||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: śarīrasya vyayena dāruṇāt tīvrād asmāt tapo-nirbandhāt nivartasva ||15||

**dīnām ekāṁ parityaktum anāthāṁ na tvam arhasi |**  
**sapatnī-vacanād vatsa agates taṁ gatir mama ||16||**

**śrīdharaḥ**: sapatnī-vacanāt kruddhaḥ san māṁ tyaktuṁ nārhasīty arthaḥ ||16||

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** kūṣmāṁḍā iti || kūṣmāṇḍāḥ-upadevabhedāḥ ||13-16|| 

**kva ca tvaṁ pañca-varṣīyaḥ kva caitad dāruṇaṁ tapaḥ |**  
**nivartyatāṁ manaḥ kaṣṭān nirbandhāt phala-varjitāt ||17||**

**kālaḥ krīḍanakānāṁ te tad-ante’dhyayanasya ca |**  
**tataḥ samasta-bhogānāṁ tad-ante ceṣyate tapaḥ ||18||**

**viṣṇucittaḥ:** kveti || nirbandhaḥ-abhiniveśaḥ ||17-18||

**mat-prītiḥ paramo dharmo vayo’vasthā-kriyā-kramam |**  
**anuvartasva sā mohaṁ nivartāsmād adharmataḥ ||19||**

**parityajati vatsādya yady etan na bhavāṁs tapaḥ |**  
**tyakṣyāmy aham api prāṇāṁs tato vai paśyatas tava ||20||**
